# Changelog

## 2026-06-15 — Bea the storyboard artist (Phase 3b) — the fleet's last named agent ($0 stub-green, TDD)

**What & why.** Phase 3 (Storyboard) had a script half (Sam) and no board half; **Bea** is the second and **last named agent in the fleet**. She reads Sam's approved `beats.json` + the Studio Brief and *proposes* a studio-voice `storyboard.md` + a **draft `shots.yaml`** (the GENERATE stage's machine input, born **unlocked**). Phase 3 is "mostly human-authored; agents assist, they don't pick beats" — Bea **proposes**, Sean curates and decides at the `storyboard approve` gate; **no critic checkpoint** at Phase-3 exit. Built standalone (like Sam / Cy's `author_bible.py`); wiring Phase 3 into `pipeline/run.py` (a `STORYBOARD` stage) is the deliberate **third slice**. **$0 at build time** — the stub fallback keeps the whole node CI-green credential-free; the real Sonnet path is written + guarded, never invoked in CI. Plan of record: [`docs/2026-06-15-bea-storyboard-build-plan.md`](docs/2026-06-15-bea-storyboard-build-plan.md) + [kickoff](docs/2026-06-15-bea-storyboard-kickoff.md). TDD, 31 new contract tests (605 → 636) + 4 eval cases; no regressions.

- **Two back-compat `shots.yaml` schema additions — [`pipeline/orchestration/shots.py`](pipeline/orchestration/shots.py).** Optional per-frame **`beat_id`** (`int | None`, validated ≥ 1 when present — the beat→shot coverage link) into `_FRAME_KEYS` + `Shot`; optional top-level **`locked`** (`bool`, default False — the curation flag) into `_TOP_KEYS` + `ShotList`. Both are **inert downstream** (`generate_stage`/`assemble_stage` never read them), so the shipped Spark `shots.yaml` (neither field) parses unchanged — `test_run_shots.py` + `test_spark_shots_equivalence.py` stay green (the back-compat proof).

- **Single-call design + the deterministic validation pass.** `StoryboardArtistNode` ([`pipeline/agents/storyboard_artist.py`](pipeline/agents/storyboard_artist.py)) makes **one** Sonnet 4.6 authoring call (`invoke_sonnet_text`, `BEA_CALL_TIMEOUT_S` default 1200s — Maya/Sam's lesson; reuses the persona-preamble-tolerant `_parse_json_envelope`), emits `storyboard.md` + a draft `shots.yaml`, then a **free deterministic pass — NOT a second LLM call** (the eval handbook bars LLM aesthetic judges; composition is the human gate's call). On a structural failure, **one re-roll** with the error threaded back (Cy's reject-reason pattern).

- **`storyboard_validate` — coverage + the script↔board conflict check.** Every beat is boarded by ≥1 shot (`beat_id == beat.id`); no shot points at a missing beat (orphans); and **every shot keeps its beat's focal cast** — `beat.cast ⊆ shot.cast`. **This direction is a deliberate correction of the kickoff's literal `shot.cast ⊆ beat.cast`** (verified against the tree, per doctrine): the real Spark board legitimately shows BOTH `sean` and the mascot in shot 3 while beat 3 ("The notice") is mascot-only, so the reverse rule would flag the shipped board. The board may *add* characters in frame (a fixed-camera two-shot), but may never *drop* a scripted one. Unlike Sam's by-ear voice defects, Bea's failure modes are **deterministic** (`beat_id` makes the link checkable).

- **Stub fallback (backward-compatible sdk_runners extension).** `invoke_sonnet_text` gained an optional `stub_fn=` param (default `_stub_sonnet_text`, so Maya's adversarial pass is byte-unchanged) — mirrors the #52 `invoke_opus_text` change. Bea passes `_make_bea_stub(sheet)`, a closure over the real beat sheet that emits **one shot per beat** (so coverage/conflict pass by construction for ANY `beats.json`) carrying the `STUB FALLBACK` marker. `scripts/author_storyboard.py`'s post-hoc `scan_stub_marker` refuses a stubbed board. `guards.py` gained `smoke_live_sonnet` (Bea authors via Sonnet, not Opus).

- **Voice — the shared instrument + the Bea-only action-line bank.** `bea-storyboard-context.md` loads `anima-standing-context.md` + the **shared, md5-stable** `sean-screenwriting-voice.md` (Sam's file, byte-unchanged) and carries Bea's "how this maps to your job" slice (the visual moves — Room-as-Biography / Loaded Object / Haptic Visuality / Metaphor-Compression) **plus the vendored Action-Line Prose Bank** (30 verbatim prose-action exemplars from [`docs/2026-06-15-bea-action-line-bank-context.md`](docs/2026-06-15-bea-action-line-bank-context.md)) — the bank lives in Bea's file only, NOT the shared voice file. A regression test asserts the §8 voice samples + the bank + the brief all reach the prompt.

- **CLI + driver.** `python -m pipeline.cli storyboard init/show/approve/mutate` ([`pipeline/cli/storyboard.py`](pipeline/cli/storyboard.py), registered in `__main__.py`) mirrors `script.py`: `show` renders a shot-list + beat-coverage tear sheet (boxes in the renderer only); **`approve` is the curation gate** — it re-validates the *curated* `shots.yaml` against `beats.json` (`load_shots` + `storyboard_validate`) and **refuses to lock a failing board**, flipping `locked: true` *textually* so the human's comments survive; `mutate` is the audited `--force`/`--actor`/`--reason` frame edit → `storyboard_audit.jsonl`. `scripts/author_storyboard.py <brief-dir> --run-dir … --manifest …` mirrors `author_script.py` (fleet-ops §0 API-key refusal + live-Sonnet smoke + the stub-marker guard). Proven end-to-end in stub mode: driver emits → the stub guard refuses; `show` renders; `approve` validates + locks.

- **Eval scaffold — [`evals/storyboard_artist/`](evals/storyboard_artist/)** (mirrors `evals/scriptwriter/`). One positive ground-truth board (the **beat_id-annotated** Spark `shots.yaml`, derived from the shipped file — NOT byte-identical, so `test_spark_shots_equivalence.py` is untouched) proves the coverage contract + Rule B. Three ships-red cases (coverage gap, orphan shot, cast conflict) are **green deterministic catches** (`storyboard_validate` raises) — not `xfail` like Sam's by-ear defects. The composition pairwise harness + the Sonnet/Gemini/Codex bake-off stay **deferred** (campaign items). `python -m pytest evals/storyboard_artist/runner.py` → 4 passed.

- **The fleet roster is now complete.** Every node of `Maya → Sam → Bea → shots.yaml → Flo/orchestrator → Em/T3 → Mo` has an agent; the human still owns the only nodes that matter (`script approve`, `storyboard approve`, the ship call). The remaining Phase-3 work is the **orchestrator-wiring slice** (the `STORYBOARD` stage in `pipeline/run.py`) — a follow-on, not a new agent. **Standing guards intact:** Em verdict-baseline `evals/vision_critic/traces/g6.1b-criteria-attached-2026-06-08.md` md5 `2af75906502f1caf8857e18828ceb2e4`, and Sam's voice file `sean-screenwriting-voice.md` md5 unchanged — both untouched by this slice.

## 2026-06-15 — Sam the scriptwriter (Phase 3a) — the first half of the fleet's last phase ($0 stub-green, TDD)

**What & why.** Phase 3 (Storyboard) had no agent; **Sam** is the first of its two — the scriptwriter. He reads Maya's `plan.md` + the Studio Brief and *proposes* a studio-voice `script.md` treatment + a structured `beats.json` beat sheet (the Sam→Bea contract). Phase 3 is "mostly human-authored; agents assist, they don't pick beats" (architecture lock + PHILOSOPHY) — Sam **proposes**, Sean decides at the `script approve` gate; there is **no critic checkpoint** at Phase-3 exit. Built standalone (like Cy's `author_bible.py`); wiring Phase 3 into `pipeline/run.py` is a deliberate follow-on after Bea. **$0 at build time** — the stub fallback keeps the whole node CI-green credential-free; the real Opus path is written + guarded, never invoked in CI. Plan of record: [`docs/2026-06-12-sam-scriptwriter-build-plan.md`](docs/2026-06-12-sam-scriptwriter-build-plan.md) + [kickoff](docs/2026-06-12-sam-scriptwriter-kickoff.md) + the [2026-06-15 screenwriting-modes addendum](docs/2026-06-15-screenwriting-modes-integration-addendum.md). TDD, 29 new tests (576 → 605); no regressions.

- **The Sam→Bea contract — [`pipeline/orchestration/beats.py`](pipeline/orchestration/beats.py)** (mirrors `shots.py`). `Beat(id, title, intent, emotional_beat, cast, feel="", notes="")` / `BeatSheet(slug, logline, beats)` / `load_beats(path, *, known_namespaces)`. Parses **JSON** (machine-emitted like `acceptance_criteria.json`, not the human-authored `shots.yaml`'s YAML) and **whitelists the top-level `locked` flag** `script approve` writes, so an approved file still reloads. `cast` uses **IR namespaces** (`sean`, `claude-mascot` — NOT the `sean-anchor` folder key), derived via `cast.derive_cast` exactly as the GENERATE stage derives `known_namespaces` for `load_shots`, so a beat's `cast` carries beat → shot → `shots.yaml` unchanged.

- **Single-call design + the deterministic structural pass.** `ScriptwriterNode` ([`pipeline/agents/scriptwriter.py`](pipeline/agents/scriptwriter.py)) makes **one** Opus 4.8 authoring call (`invoke_opus_text`, `SAM_CALL_TIMEOUT_S` default 1200s — Maya's lesson; reuses her persona-preamble-tolerant `_parse_json_envelope`), then a **free deterministic structural pass — NOT a second LLM call.** The eval handbook bars LLM aesthetic judges on creative quality (weak/self-preferring); the taste call is the human gate. Maya's Opus→Sonnet adversarial second pass makes sense for a *graph* artifact (criteria) — Sam outputs prose + a beat list, where the failure mode that matters (surface pastiche vs. real stylistic-mechanism modeling) only a deep model avoids and only Sean's ear can fix.

- **Coverage re-defined — cast-coverage, not "plan.md story points" (Decision #1, Sean-ratified 2026-06-15).** The kickoff/build-plan framed the structural pass as catching a "coverage gap against plan.md story points." Free-prose story-point matching needs an LLM, which v1 bars. **The deterministic red failure class is a cast-coverage gap** (a loaded character with no beat). `structural_validate` checks: every loaded character in ≥1 beat + ids strictly ascending + beat count in [3, 12] + arc-presence (emotional beats not all identical). Narrative fidelity is the human gate's call (PHILOSOPHY: agents propose, the human decides). *This supersedes the "story-point coverage" framing in the build plan's build-order step 2 + acceptance criterion — update those when the planning docs are committed.*

- **Voice — full vendored instrument, not a condensed note (per the 2026-06-15 addendum).** [`pipeline/agents/prompts/sean-screenwriting-voice.md`](pipeline/agents/prompts/sean-screenwriting-voice.md) is the **verbatim** vendor of the code-brain `screenwriting-modes` skill (md5-pinned provenance header; shared — Bea loads it too). The original plan called for a condensed "Sean's register" note; the skill's own anti-distillation contract says voice doesn't survive distillation — the §8 verbatim samples are the load-bearing part. `pipeline/agents/prompts/sam-scriptwriter-context.md` is Sam's role addendum; `scriptwriter.py` loads `anima-standing-context.md` + the addendum + the voice instrument (a regression test asserts the §8 samples reach the prompt).

- **Stub fallback (backward-compatible sdk_runners extension).** `invoke_opus_text` gained an optional `stub_fn=` param (default `_stub_opus_text`, so Maya/Cy are byte-unchanged); Sam passes `_stub_sam_text`, which emits a Sam-shaped `{script_md, beats_json}` envelope carrying the `STUB FALLBACK` marker. `scripts/author_script.py`'s post-hoc `scan_stub_marker` (the shared guard) refuses a stubbed script — a stub can never silently pass the human gate.

- **CLI + driver.** `python -m pipeline.cli script init/show/approve/mutate` ([`pipeline/cli/script.py`](pipeline/cli/script.py), registered in `__main__.py` next to `plan`/`bible`/`patches`) mirrors `plan.py`: `show` renders a beat-sheet tear sheet (box-drawing in the renderer only — `beats.json` on disk stays clean); `approve` flips `locked: true` idempotently (symlink-safe); `mutate` is the audited `--force`/`--actor`/`--reason` beat-field edit → `runs/{id}/script_audit.jsonl`. `scripts/author_script.py <brief-dir> --run-dir … --manifest …` mirrors `author_plan.py` (fleet-ops §0 API-key refusal + live-Opus smoke + the stub-marker guard).

- **Eval scaffold — [`evals/scriptwriter/`](evals/scriptwriter/)** (mirrors `evals/planner/`; the pairwise-preference harness stays **deferred** — campaign item). Two positive ground-truth cases validate beats round-trip + structural pass: `spark-shared` (the real anima brief, plumbing/coverage) and `figgy-pudding` (the 2026-06-15 Sean-ratified voice dry-run, a dialogue-heavy exemplar with its own `greta`/`doug` namespaces so it round-trips in isolation; voice *quality* not asserted — structure only). Six ships-red anti-pattern cases (SR-1 narrator-quip, SR-2 register-collapse, theme-spoken, naked-tender-pivot, clean-catharsis, recycled-coffee-prop) seed the deferred harness: 5 by-ear defects → `xfail` (Decision #2 — SR-1 is **not** regex-deterministic; documented gaps, no detector built); the 1 literal default-prop case is caught by the eval-side `default_prop_lint` (the sanctioned deterministic exception). `python -m pytest evals/scriptwriter/runner.py` → 3 passed, 5 xfailed.

- **Phase 3 is now half-built.** Bea (`storyboard_artist`, the board half) + the `pipeline/run.py` STORYBOARD-stage wiring remain (follow-on slices). The `beats.py` contract is proven against a real authored beat sheet so Bea is built against a hardened, not hypothetical, handoff. **Verdict-baseline guard intact:** `evals/vision_critic/traces/g6.1b-criteria-attached-2026-06-08.md` md5 `2af75906502f1caf8857e18828ceb2e4`, untouched.

## 2026-06-15 — Phase 3 voice integration: `screenwriting-modes` skill → Sam/Bea (planning + vendored artifact, $0, no code)

**What & why.** Sean's `screenwriting-modes` skill (the screen twin of `writing-voice-modes`) now exists in `code-brain`, built specifically so the Phase 3 agents write in his voice. This session integrates it at the planning layer — no agent code yet (the Sam build still runs via its kickoff under fleet-ops discipline). Two new docs + pointer patches:

- **`docs/2026-06-15-sam-bea-screenwriting-voice-context.md`** — the **ready-to-vendor full voice instrument** (anti-distillation contract + 6 modes native→trap + the signature-moves table + the WHAT/taste layers + the §8 verbatim samples + anti-patterns). The build session vendors it verbatim to `pipeline/agents/prompts/sean-screenwriting-voice.md`, loaded by both `sam-scriptwriter-context.md` and (later) `bea-storyboard-context.md` — same pattern as the shared `anima-standing-context.md`. Carries a provenance header + re-sync trigger (cross-repo vendor; canonical source stays the code-brain skill).
- **`docs/2026-06-15-screenwriting-modes-integration-addendum.md`** — the 6 integration points and the correction it makes: the original Sam plan (2026-06-12) deferred the voice layer to "a condensed register note" because the skill lived in another repo / didn't exist. That's now superseded — Sam vendors the **full** instrument, because the skill's own anti-distillation contract (*voice doesn't survive distillation; exemplars drive*) makes a condensed note the exact failure mode, which is also Sam's named #1 risk (surface pastiche). Sean ratified full-fidelity vendoring 2026-06-15.

**Also captured:** the skill's anti-patterns become near-binary **ships-red** eval cases for `evals/scriptwriter/` (theme-spoken, recycled-prop, naked-tender-pivot, clean-catharsis, narrator-voice-cheese) — sharper than beat-coverage, no quality-judge needed; the **Sam→Bea seam is now concrete** (the Room-as-Biography / Loaded-Object move — Sam writes the object, Bea boards it — also a candidate Bea Opus-escalation trigger); the `script-writing` structural spines (therefore/but, want-engine, kishotenketsu, trope-autopsy, Declare-then-Puncture) inform the beat sheet.

**Pointer patches (so the build can't build the wrong thing):** banners added atop the [brainstorm](docs/2026-06-12-sam-bea-phase3-brainstorm.md), [build plan](docs/2026-06-12-sam-scriptwriter-build-plan.md), and [kickoff](docs/2026-06-12-sam-scriptwriter-kickoff.md); kickoff build-order step 3 + the build-plan file map amended from "condensed register note" to the full vendor. The four locked forks, the `beats.py` contract, the single-call/deterministic-pass design, Sam-first sequencing, and the $0/TDD/stub-green discipline are **all unchanged**. No code touched; `evals/vision_critic/` untouched.

**Voice validated + eval seed captured (same day).** A live dry-run of the vendored instrument (fresh code-brain session, Sean-supplied premise — a Christmas-caroler dessert-siege, NOT the buy-from-a-clerk rut) was **ratified by Sean**: the skill read its §8 exemplars first, led with the WHAT layer, built an earned (not stapled) emotional anchor, clawed the win through an escalating obstacle ladder, and landed a dirty-victory/callback closer with no spoken theme. The run also surfaced two ships-red eval negatives (SR-1 narrator-grade meta-quip in a character's mouth; SR-2 register-contrast collapse / two-clever-people — the by-ear failure a checklist under-catches). Captured build-ready as the scriptwriter eval seed at [`docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-15-screenwriting-voice-dry-run-and-eval-seed.md`](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-15-screenwriting-voice-dry-run-and-eval-seed.md) (the validated "Figgy Pudding" run as the positive voice case + SR-1/SR-2). The 2026-06-15 dry-run refinements (coffee/default-prop ban, earned-anchor rule, clawed-win rule) were folded into the canonical skill and mirrored into the vendored copy. Sam build is green-to-go: `origin/main` at `742b629` (#51, the kickoff's expected baseline).

## 2026-06-11 — Run orchestrator Slice 2.1: pre-costed hardening ($0 stub-green, TDD) — `--stub` walks brief→loop offline; the brief is never clobbered

**What & why.** Two audit findings made the orchestrator unprovable-without-spending, plus one the live smoke surfaced mid-slice. Plan of record: [`docs/2026-06-11-orchestrator-hardening-2.1-build-plan.md`](docs/2026-06-11-orchestrator-hardening-2.1-build-plan.md) + [kickoff](docs/2026-06-11-orchestrator-hardening-2.1-kickoff.md) (both committed with this slice); field report: [`docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-11-orchestrator-hardening-2.1-field-report.md`](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-11-orchestrator-hardening-2.1-field-report.md). Three independent TDD commits, each revertible alone:

- **Fix B — brief snapshot (`pipeline/run.py:_start`).** The PLAN stage wrote `plan.md`/`acceptance_criteria.json`/`01_production_brief.md` into the *committed* brief dir and `--approve-plan` locked the brief's criteria in place (the audit clobbered `briefs/2026-06-10-spark-shared/`, restored from HEAD). `_start` now `copytree`s the brief → `run_dir/brief/` and points `state.brief_dir`/`state.shots_path` at the run-local copy — every downstream site reads state, so one site changed. New optional `brief_src` state field keeps provenance (`--status` shows `brief: …/brief (snapshot of briefs/…)`; the Maya gate print uses the source name). **Residual:** `scripts/author_plan.py` (the manual escape hatch) still writes into the brief dir it's given — the snapshot protects only `python -m pipeline.run`.
- **Fix A — `flo_stub` offline placeholder (`pipeline/agents/flo_stub.py` + the switch in `generate_stage.run_frame_fan`).** `--stub` stubbed Maya but not Flo's image transport, so a live `--stub` run died at F01 (`flo F01 nb2 route returned no candidate`) — the held costed run would have been the first time the CLI ever chained GENERATE→ASSEMBLE. The new node writes a real 1376×768 PNG (clears HF01 at 0.78% deviation; bytes vary per attempt so re-rolls get fresh Em cache keys); `run_frame_fan` selects it on the persisted run-level `state["stub"]`. Node id stays `flo_{fid}`; `node_name` is in the DAG cache key, so stub/real results can never cross-serve. **Headline proof:** a production-path integration test (no flo monkeypatch — env shaping only) drives the real `pipeline.run.main()` PLAN → approve-plan → approve every frame → ASSEMBLE → **DONE** with `GEMINI_API_KEY` unset, loop files on disk, `[stub]` in `--status`.
- **Force-stub gate — `ANIMA_FORCE_STUB` (out-of-plan, surfaced by the live smoke).** The build plan's locked semantics said "`--stub` stubs Maya's plan" — but verify-against-the-tree showed Maya (and Em) went **live** under `--stub` whenever a transport was reachable: `claude-agent-sdk` importable (subscription OAuth, no key needed) or `GEMINI_API_KEY` in env **or the project `.env`** (`gemini_api_runner._resolve_gemini_key` reads it). The first in-session smoke had to be killed mid-flight to honor the $0 doctrine — the inverse of the silent-stub trap: silent SPEND. `pipeline.run` now exports `ANIMA_FORCE_STUB=1` for the dynamic extent of a `--stub` invocation (set in `_start`/`_resume`, restored in `main()`'s `finally` so in-process callers never leak it); all three model-transport gates honor it (`sdk_runners._sdk_available`, `gemini_api_runner.run_gemini_api_with_image`, `cli_runners.run_antigravity_with_image`). A non-stub run never sets it; a manually exported flag fails closed via Maya's stub-marker guard.

**Test-boundary migration (the spec's "existing suite stays green" was false as written).** Every orchestrator CLI test runs `--stub` (the stub-marker guard forces it) while faking `pipeline.generate.generate_frame` — a boundary the Fix A switch bypasses, so 8 test sites broke or went *vacuously green* (the interrupt-recovery test's flaky fake would simply never fire). Migrated to the `flo_stub` boundary: new `tests/orch_fixtures.spy_flo_stub` (same call-dict shape as `fake_flo_generate`); the errored-attempt and interrupt tests now raise from `FloStubNode.run`; real-`flo` dispatch + seam #11 (FOLDER key) stay covered by a new parametrized `run_frame_fan` switch test driving the fan directly with `stub=False`.

**Honesty notes.** A stub run is labeled at every surface (`[stub]` on stage + plan lines; placeholder candidates). Hand-editing `run_state.json` to flip `stub` would let placeholders count as real attempts — manual tamper, accepted, not coded against. Live smoke (plain documented command, SDK installed, $0): `--brief briefs/2026-06-10-spark-shared --stub` → DONE, exports built over placeholders, `git status -s briefs/` + `git diff briefs/` **empty** — the committed spark brief byte-unchanged through a full run against it.

**Counts & guards.** `tests/` 562 → **576** (+2 snapshot, +3 flo_stub unit, +1 production-path offline, +2 switch, +6 force-stub); `pipeline/tests/` 10 green; Slice 1 PT_A1 golden + Slice 2's orchestrator tests green (migrated, intent preserved). Fleet-ops: isolated worktree off `origin/main` `dea68e3`, divergence `0 0`, `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` absent. **Em's verdict baseline `evals/vision_critic/traces/g6.1b-criteria-attached-2026-06-08.md` (`md5 2af75906502f1caf8857e18828ceb2e4`) byte-identical** — `evals/vision_critic/` untouched. Kickoff deltas recorded in the field report (orchestrator test count was 36 not 41; the ".env present → 2 `test_frame_router` failures" note didn't reproduce; baseline was 562 passed / 0 skipped, not 560/2). Out of scope held: the costed run, seam #10 (Em CC01), seam #14 (museum, Slice 3).

## 2026-06-11 — Run orchestrator Slice 2: the CORE BUILD ($0 stub-green, TDD) — `python -m pipeline.run` exists

**What & why.** The one-command chainer that turns the first integrated run's **16 hand-wired joins into a single resumable program**. Plan of record: [`docs/2026-06-11-orchestrator-core-build-plan.md`](docs/2026-06-11-orchestrator-core-build-plan.md) (committed with this slice, with its kickoff); seam spec: [`docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-11-first-integrated-run.md`](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-11-first-integrated-run.md). The load-bearing finding held against the tree: `pipeline/dag.py`'s `Runner.execute` is a **batch executor** (a raising node propagates immediately; no pause/resume), so the orchestrator is a **resumable stage machine** (`PLAN → GENERATE → ASSEMBLE → DONE`, durable `runs/<id>/run_state.json`, exits at every human gate) that uses the Runner only for small static sub-graphs. **$0 — every transport stubbed/faked; the costed end-to-end validation is a separate out-of-session step (plain terminal, seam #4).** Executed under [`docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md`](docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md): isolated worktree off `origin/main` `ec81cf0`, `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` absent, divergence `0 0` before, TDD red→green per phase. **Em's verdict baseline `evals/vision_critic/traces/g6.1b-criteria-attached-2026-06-08.md` (`md5 2af75906502f1caf8857e18828ceb2e4`) byte-identical** — `evals/vision_critic/` untouched. Museum capture (seam #14) is Slice 3; Em CC01 (seam #10) stays eval-gated.
- **The CLI + state machine** ([`pipeline/run.py`](pipeline/run.py) + [`pipeline/orchestration/`](pipeline/orchestration/)): `--brief <dir>` (derive cast, drive Maya behind the extracted guards, stop at the plan gate) → `--resume <run-dir> --approve-plan` (lock criteria via the same `pipeline.cli plan approve` code path, wire `criteria_sources.brief_file` **in-memory** from state on every invocation — `manifest.yaml` on disk never edited — build the merged bundle once via `load_all_criteria`, enter GENERATE, fan frame 1) → per-frame eye gates (`--approve-frame N [--attempt K]` locks → `approved/<slug>_F0N_key.png` + chains N+1 off the **approved** prior; `--retry-frame N --note` re-rolls with spark's exact `CORRECTION (re-roll, …)` line) → ASSEMBLE auto-runs after the last approval (`--assemble` retries a failed tail) → DONE. `--status` renders state without advancing; `--stub` is the explicit $0 smoke mode (skips the live-Opus smoke, records `plan.stub: true` — a stub plan is never silently real; without it the STUB-marker scan hard-fails, seam #1's silent-stub trap). State writes are atomic (serialize-first, tmp+replace); every `--resume` is a fresh process against the durable file, so a laptop close mid-run loses nothing (P4's interrupt test proves it).
- **The per-frame fan runs through the DAG Runner — the recommended path, not the fallback (seam #7 dissolved).** Per frame: an in-memory `flo_fNN → audit_fNN` graph, then one `em_fNN_<ns>` single-node graph per cast namespace, all on ONE Runner with `add_hook("post_run", stage_patches_hook)` — **Em's patches stage for free**. The split (not one big graph) is deliberate: `execute` aborts wholesale on a raising node, and Em's `EmptyCitesInvariant` is a *recoverable per-namespace verdict* (recorded as `human_review (empty-cites invariant)`, the other namespace still runs — spark-faithful), while a Flo/audit crash records an **honest errored attempt** (`errored:` in state, rc 1, recover via `--retry-frame`). Verified, not assumed: a cache-hit `post_run` re-fire is **patch-less by construction** (the sidecar doesn't persist `proposed_patches`), so resume can't double-stage; state-first idempotency (a recorded attempt is never re-fanned) is the primary guard anyway.
- **The attempt salt — same-note retries genuinely re-roll.** Flo's output path comes from `generate_frame`'s attempt-counting glob; the content-addressed cache would make a same-note retry a silent fake re-roll (same prompt + refs → same key → cached candidate). The Flo node now carries `config={"attempt": k}` — config participates in the cache key — so a retry is always a real generation while a resume of the same attempt is an idempotent cache hit.
- **`Runner` gained two additive kwargs (the only `dag.py` edit, fully back-compat):** `criteria_bundle=` (a pre-built MERGED bundle — brief AC.* + every Bible's IR.* — reaches every node's `ctx.criteria`; the single-`criteria` Path form is byte-identical otherwise) + `criteria_hash=` (paired with `generate_stage.combined_criteria_hash`, which hashes ALL `criteria_sources` files so a mutation in any of them still invalidates downstream cache).
- **Seams #9 + #11 — the `character_id` dual meaning, threaded from one table.** `orchestration/cast.derive_cast` builds `state.cast` once at run init: folder keys from manifest `characters:`, IR namespace by **loading** each Bible's criteria and reading the validator-enforced `character_id` field (no string parsing; >1 namespace per Bible = config error; a Bible-less character only errors when a shot casts it). Flo receives the folder key (`style_register` routing), Em the namespace (`query_by_character`) — pinned by a spy test at both node boundaries.
- **`shots.yaml` — the externalized FRAMES dict (the input contract).** The brief dir now carries the human-authored shot list (`orchestration/shots.py`: `slug` + per frame `id`/`cast` (IR namespaces, first = primary)/`beat`/`prompt`/`extra_references`/`chain_anchors` (⊆ cast, default all)/`hold` (default 2, on-twos); strict validation — unknown keys, non-ascending ids, unknown namespaces all refuse). [`briefs/2026-06-10-spark-shared/shots.yaml`](briefs/2026-06-10-spark-shared/shots.yaml) was **generated verbatim** from `spark_frame.FRAMES` and is the costed-validation input; `tests/test_spark_shots_equivalence.py` pins prompts/beats/plates AND the reference recipe (F01 = both anchors + A-7; F0N = approved-first + approved-prior + chain anchors + the beat's plate, deduped) against the prototype — **"don't fork" enforced by golden test**; `scripts/spark_frame.py` itself stays untouched as the manual escape hatch. `scripts/author_plan.py` was rewired onto the extracted [`orchestration/guards.py`](pipeline/orchestration/guards.py) (`smoke_live_opus` + `scan_stub_marker`), behavior-identical.
- **ASSEMBLE tail:** `export/sequence.txt` written from `frame_order` + `holds` (full-basename `KEY:hold` lines), driven through the Slice-1-generalized `assemble.sh` via `AssembleNode` (`--slug` + `--sequence-file`), consuming the #12-normalized PNGs; loop paths recorded in state. Slice 1's golden PT_A1 byte-identical test stays green.
- **Tests.** Contract suite 521 → **562** (`python -m pytest tests/`; +41: state 8, plan/cast/shots 15, dag-bundle 3, generate-fan 8, spark-equivalence 2, assemble 3, integration 2), Seedance **10** — both green credential-free. Stub-test honesty note: Em's stub path always escalates (gemini stub borderline@0.65 < the 0.7 threshold → opus stub borderline@0.78, cites `AC01`), and fan tests fake Flo with REAL 1376×768 PNGs because `audit.check_aspect_ratio` PIL-opens candidates uncaught.
- **Next (out of session, fleet-ops §0):** the costed validation — `python -m pipeline.run --brief briefs/2026-06-10-spark-shared` from a **plain terminal** (~$0.66-ish). Note for that run: the shipped Spark loop had **6** keys (`SS_F03b` peak insert); the 5-frame shots.yaml reproduces the 5-key cut — the peak insert stays a hand edit to `sequence.txt`.

## 2026-06-11 — Run orchestrator Slice 1: the cleanup pass ($0, TDD) — 3 seam fixes, each red→green

**What & why.** Slice 1 of the run-orchestrator build (plan of record: [`docs/2026-06-11-run-orchestrator-build-plan.md`](docs/2026-06-11-run-orchestrator-build-plan.md); kickoff: [`docs/2026-06-11-orchestrator-cleanup-pass-kickoff.md`](docs/2026-06-11-orchestrator-cleanup-pass-kickoff.md)). Three independent seams the [first integrated run](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-11-first-integrated-run.md) logged — fixed as pure code + unit tests, **no model spend**, so the Slice-2 orchestrator builds on a clean base. Each is its own red→green commit, revertible alone. Executed under [`docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md`](docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md): isolated worktree off `origin/main` `f157564`, `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` absent, divergence `0 0` before. **Em's verdict baseline `evals/vision_critic/traces/g6.1b-criteria-attached-2026-06-08.md` (`md5 2af75906502f1caf8857e18828ceb2e4`) byte-identical** — `evals/vision_critic/` untouched (seam #10, Em's stylus-hand verdict, is held OUT as a separate eval-gated track).
- **#5 — cost estimator double-counted locked Bibles.** [`cost_estimator._phase_2_cost`](pipeline/agents/cost_estimator.py) priced every non-`ingest:` plate from each registered character's `plate_generation_plan.json` and only zeroed when there was *no* `characters:` block. An `animation_piece` registers its Bibles to load references, and both shipped Bibles (`sean-anchor`, `claude-mascot`) are `locked: true` — so it billed a phantom Phase-2 band for a bake it never does. **Real locked-Bible manifest: $5.40/$16.20 → $0.00.** A locked Bible is already authored (load-only); new `_bible_locked(folder)` reads the per-Bible `acceptance_criteria.json` `locked: true` directly (the same flag `bible approve` flips) and skips it. A character with no lock file / `locked: false` prices its plates exactly as today (genuine authoring estimate preserved). +2 tests.
- **#12 — Gemini saved JPEG-as-`.png`.** The pencil skill writes JPEG bytes under an `attempt_NN.png` name (the run's `SS_F01_key.png` is "JPEG image data … 1376x768"); ffmpeg's PNG decoder drops them and the future museum capture would copy a mislabeled thumbnail. Fixed at the source: new [`pipeline/agents/image_utils.normalize_to_png(path)`](pipeline/agents/image_utils.py) (PIL: re-encode in place iff `format != PNG`; returns whether it rewrote) runs at both [`FloNode.run`](pipeline/agents/frame_router.py) return sites, so Em / assemble / museum all receive a real PNG. Defensive on the per-frame hot path — a file PIL can't open is passed through (returns False), never crashes the node; idempotent no-op on an already-PNG file. `assemble.sh` Step 2b stays as the backstop. +4 tests.
- **#13 — `assemble.sh` hardcoded to PT_A1.** It baked in the 27-entry `FRAME_SEQ`, the `PT_A1_` source prefix, and the `pencil-test-act1` output slug. Generalized with two optional flags defaulting to today's behavior: `--sequence-file <path>` (same `KEY:hold` format; full-basename keys → empty source prefix) and `--slug <name>`. [`AssembleNode`](pipeline/nodes/assemble.py) threads optional `slug` / `sequence_file` inputs to the flags (absent → bare legacy argv) so Slice 2 can drive an arbitrary piece. Scale (1920×1080) and Step 2b unchanged. +4 hermetic tests (fake-ffmpeg PATH shim; assert on the staged `export/sequence/` + planned names, no real encode); the **golden back-compat test locks the PT_A1 staged frame→source digest (`sha256 70a977a2…`) and is green before AND after the change** — the byte-identical proof, mirroring Flo-C's NB-Pro cache-key digest lock.
- **Tests.** Contract suite 511 → **521** (`python -m pytest tests/`), Seedance 10 (`python -m pytest pipeline/tests/`), both green.

## 2026-06-11 — Run orchestrator SCOPED + sliced (planning, $0): 4 forks resolved, cleanup-pass kickoff written

**What & why.** Scoped the **run orchestrator** — the one major fleet member still missing — off the first integrated run's 16-seam field report ([`docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-11-first-integrated-run.md`](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-11-first-integrated-run.md)). Planning only; no code, no spend. The load-bearing finding (verified against the tree, not the prompt): **`pipeline/dag.py`'s `Runner` is a batch executor with no pause/resume** — so the orchestrator is a standalone, resumable **stage machine** that *owns* the human gates and the per-frame loop and *uses* the DAG Runner only for the genuinely-static tails (the per-frame Flo→T1→Em fan, assemble→museum). The Phase-5 per-frame gate (eye + retry, each frame chained off the *approved* prior) is **not expressible as a static DAG** — that's the new mechanism.
- **Four strategy forks resolved with Sean.** (1) **Slicing:** cleanup pass first, then core. (2) **Run context:** standalone shell, uncontended — the orchestrator runs from a plain shell so heavy Opus nodes (Maya, T3) dodge the ~285–390s nested-SDK throttle (seam #4 + the stalled T3 gate, same root cause). (3) **Museum #14:** defer until after core. (4) **Gate UX:** durable state file + `--resume` (survives a laptop close; pairs with standalone execution). Seam **#10** (Em stylus-hand in profile) is held OUT of every cleanup slice — it changes Em's verdicts and carries eval-baseline blast radius; separate eval-gated track.
- **Slice 1 = cleanup pass ($0, TDD), grounded against the tree.** **#5** `cost_estimator._phase_2_cost` prices every plate regardless of lock state → phantom ~$5.40 Phase-2 band on `animation_piece` runs against locked Bibles (both `sean-anchor` + `claude-mascot` carry `locked: true`); fix = skip locked Bibles. **#12** `SS_F01_key.png` is JPEG-data-as-`.png` (ffmpeg PNG-decode fails) → normalize at the `FloNode.run` return boundary (source fix), keep `assemble.sh` Step 2b as backstop. **#13** `assemble.sh` hardcodes the PT_A1 `FRAME_SEQ` + `PT_A1_` prefix + `pencil-test-act1` output names → generalize to accept a sequence spec + `--slug`, PT_A1 stays byte-identical (golden test).
- **Artifacts (Cowork-authored).** Build plan [`docs/2026-06-11-run-orchestrator-build-plan.md`](docs/2026-06-11-run-orchestrator-build-plan.md) (full 3-slice arc + the seam→slice traceability for all 16 seams) and the paste-ready Slice-1 kickoff [`docs/2026-06-11-orchestrator-cleanup-pass-kickoff.md`](docs/2026-06-11-orchestrator-cleanup-pass-kickoff.md). Next Claude Code session executes Slice 1 under fleet-ops. **Em's verdict baseline `evals/vision_critic/traces/g6.1b-criteria-attached-2026-06-08.md` (`md5 2af75906502f1caf8857e18828ceb2e4`) untouched** — planning only.

A best-effort `maya_raw_pass1.txt` dump was added for evidence.

## 2026-06-10 — Flo, Session C ($0 stub-green): Flo is now the DISPATCHED Phase-5 node + HF01 fixed on the NB Pro path

**What & why.** Flo-A (#43) built the router and Flo-B (#44) chose the in-between routes, but **Flo was registered, not dispatched** — no run actually chained through `FloNode`; the only consumer was the registration import. Session C makes Flo the **dispatched** Phase-5 generation node via the declarative DAG path, threads the routing signals onto frame specs, and fixes the HF01 square-frame bug on the NB Pro keyframe path — the two prerequisites for the first integrated end-to-end run. Plan of record: [`docs/2026-06-10-flo-router-build-plan.md`](docs/2026-06-10-flo-router-build-plan.md); kickoff: [`docs/2026-06-10-flo-router-session-c-kickoff.md`](docs/2026-06-10-flo-router-session-c-kickoff.md). Builds on Flo-A (#43) + Flo-B (#44). Executed under [`docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md`](docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md): isolated worktree off `origin/main` `3659032`, `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` absent (no spend — stub-green throughout), divergence `0 0` before, TDD red→green per step.
- **C0 — the gap confirmed against the tree (not the doc).** `grep '"flo"|FloNode|resolve_route'` hit only `frame_router.py` + the registration import in [`pipeline/nodes/__init__.py`](pipeline/nodes/__init__.py) — nothing dispatched `flo`. The declarative dispatch mechanism **already existed**: [`dag.py:load_graph_from_manifest`](pipeline/dag.py) reads `phases.*.nodes[*]` and dispatches whatever `node:` names, and `run_from_legacy_cli` **ignores** the `node_id="frame_generate"` arg [`generate.py:main()`](pipeline/generate.py) passes (vestigial). So wiring `flo` needed **no change to `generate.py`** — a worked `phases.phase_5.nodes` graph + input bindings. [`nb_pro_runner._build_skill_cmd`](pipeline/agents/nb_pro_runner.py) built the skill argv with **no `--aspect-ratio`** → the skill defaults to 1:1 → fails [`audit.check_aspect_ratio`](pipeline/audit.py) (16:9 ±2%); only the `nb_pro` routes were affected (the `nb2` path goes through `generate_frame`, which already passes `--aspect-ratio 16:9`).
- **C1 — `literal_json:` binding form (the impedance fix, TDD).** [`dag.py:_resolve_bindings`](pipeline/dag.py) supported only `literal:` (string), `node:`, `manifest:` — no way to bind a list-valued `references` inline on a node entry. Added a `literal_json:` form that JSON-parses the spec → supports list/int/bool inputs (e.g. FloNode's `references`), with a clear `ValueError` on malformed JSON. Additive; the three legacy forms are untouched (regression-locked). +7 tests in [`tests/test_dag.py`](tests/test_dag.py).
- **C2/C3 — `flo` dispatched declaratively + `shot_type`/`character_id` threaded.** A `phases.phase_5.nodes` graph whose entries carry `node: flo` now dispatches through the DAG runner; bindings supply `frame_num`/`prompt`/`references`/`shot_type`/`character_id` so routing is **real** (hero→NB Pro, standard→NB2; `style_register` resolved from the named character). The worked example lives at [`docs/examples/flo-phase5-example.yaml`](docs/examples/flo-phase5-example.yaml) — the seam Maya's run session builds on — **not** baked into production `manifest.yaml` (authoring the real scene graph is the run session's job; production `phases:` stays `enabled: []`, so a real run is byte-identical). The legacy `frame_generate` node is untouched; the kickoff's "FrameGenerateNode delegation" fallback was **rejected** (declarative dispatch works; delegation would conflate the two nodes). Back-compat: no `generation.routing:` block → `resolve_route` returns `None` → legacy single-model fall-through.
- **C4 — HF01 fixed on the NB Pro path (TDD).** Added `aspect_ratio: str | None = None` to [`invoke_image_edit`](pipeline/agents/nb_pro_runner.py) + `_build_skill_cmd` (appends `--aspect-ratio <ratio>` **only when set**), and Flo's `nb_pro` dispatch branch ([`frame_router.py`](pipeline/agents/frame_router.py)) passes `aspect_ratio="16:9"` so hero_keyframe + in_between_mid clear HF01. **Cy regression-locked:** `aspect_ratio` folds into the cache key **only when non-None**, so Cy's locked-Bible plate calls + the proportion-gate call (which pass no `aspect_ratio`) keep a **byte-identical argv + cache key** — verified against a captured pre-change golden digest `7a84b913…4258d`. +4 tests in [`tests/test_nb_pro_runner.py`](tests/test_nb_pro_runner.py) + 1 in [`tests/test_frame_router.py`](tests/test_frame_router.py).
- **C5 — stub-green integration smoke + green.** New `test_flo_phase5_graph_dispatches_via_dag` in [`tests/test_dag.py`](tests/test_dag.py): a declared two-node `flo` graph (hero→nb_pro, standard→nb2, references via `literal_json:`) dispatches through `load_graph_from_manifest` → `Runner.execute` with both transports faked — proves declarative dispatch, real-list reference binding, 16:9 on the nb_pro path, and the route-in-`notes`, **no real call fires**. The example manifest is **not** run live (its nb2 node would either abort without a key or spend with one — both wrong for $0); a read-only graph-load confirms it parses. Full contract suite [`tests/`](tests/) **506 passed**, [`pipeline/tests/`](pipeline/tests/) **10 passed**. **Em's verdict baseline `traces/g6.1b-criteria-attached-2026-06-08.md` (`md5 2af75906502f1caf8857e18828ceb2e4`) byte-identical** — `evals/vision_critic/` untouched; Flo-B's in-between decision (nb2/nb_pro) unchanged.
- **Out of scope (the run session):** authoring the real Sean-+-mascot scene graph, the Maya brief/plan, the costed generation, the Em/T3 critique pass, assembly, museum capture. Session C is the $0 wiring that makes those possible.
- **Field report + post-mortem (added 2026-06-10, post-merge):** [`docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-10-flo-router-session-c.md`](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-10-flo-router-session-c.md) records the $0 outcome and a retrospective on an **operational incident** — early test edits leaked to the **main-repo path instead of the worktree** (reused pre-worktree absolute paths after `EnterWorktree` switched cwd). Caught by the **"wrong test-collection count" tell** (`-k` deselected all 7 new tests → only the original 10 collected), restored main pristine with `git checkout`, re-applied against the worktree path; no main-branch pollution shipped. Prevention captured: after `EnterWorktree` the worktree path is the only valid edit root; treat a surprising collection/test count as an isolation tell; spot-check `git -C <main-repo> status -s` after the first worktree edit. Same incident class as the 2026-06-02 fleet-ops adoption — "one isolated worktree per plan" only protects you if every mutation lands *in* it.

## 2026-06-10 — Flo, Session B (B0 + smoke + DECISION, ~$0.58): fal endpoints verified LIVE → NB2 pivot (Sean's eye disqualified both fal candidates)

**What & why.** Ran the costed half of Flo-B and **decided**: pencil in-betweens **pivot to NB2** (winner) + **NB Pro** (backup). The question was whether a fal.ai image-edit model preserves grain AND identity through an in-between well enough to wire as Flo's `in_between_*` route. **Answer: no** — Sean's eye disqualified both candidates on the live smoke, exactly reproducing the 2026-06-08 Reve finding (a model can score well on grain/embedding yet **morph the character identity through the tween**, which is fatal for in-betweens and invisible to DINOv2). The full 4×14 run was deliberately **not** run — the smoke was decisive (Engine Truth). Executed under [`docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md`](docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md): isolated worktree off `origin/main` `112a99b`, `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` absent (Em never invoked), `FAL_KEY`/`GEMINI_API_KEY` bounded from the worktree `.env`, §0 before AND after, orphan sweep clean. Decision artifact: [`evals/bakeoffs/2026-06-10-flo-inbetween-pencil-pilot/results.md`](evals/bakeoffs/2026-06-10-flo-inbetween-pencil-pilot/results.md); field report: [`docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-10-flo-inbetween-pencil-pilot.md`](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-10-flo-inbetween-pencil-pilot.md).
- **STEP B0 — both fal transports verified LIVE** (the reve mirror-schema lesson, applied: [`fal_runner.py`](pipeline/agents/fal_runner.py) shipped the endpoint ids as unverified candidates that REFUSE the real path until verified). Verified against the live fal OpenAPI (first-party) + confirming single probes (real 1376×768 outputs): **Seedream** `fal-ai/bytedance/seedream/v4/edit` (candidate id correct); **Qwen CORRECTED** to `fal-ai/qwen-image-edit-plus` — the base `qwen-image-edit` takes a single image, unusable for a two-endpoint tween; **no `denoise`/`strength` knob is exposed** (the kickoff's 0.78–0.82 sweet-spot is not real on this endpoint — ran at fal defaults). Both default to a **square** output → forced to the 16:9 source-frame size. `verified=True` for both; `variants.yaml snapshots:` pinned; the refusal mechanism still tested by forcing `verified=False` (+1 regression test, 9 total).
- **2-case live smoke (~$0.53, 8 real frames):** 4 variants × 2 cases (transition F01→F06, IB at 25% + 50%). **Verdict (Sean's eye):** **nb2 = winner** (holds identity + pencil register), **nb-pro = backup**; **fal-seedream = disqualified** ("close", strong grain, but **morphs the face** — the Reve trap); **fal-qwen-plus = disqualified** ("terrible" — reframes/zooms, composition instability).

The deferred `mask_edit` (gpt_image_2) remains the lone not-wired seam. [`tests/test_frame_router.py`](tests/test_frame_router.py): +1 positive pivot test (`…in_between_pivot_routes_to_wired_nb_transports`); the old `in_between_cheap`-based not-wired + lowered-confidence tests repointed to `mask_edit`/`gpt_image_2`. The **verified** fal transports stay in [`fal_runner.py`](pipeline/agents/fal_runner.py) (retained for future **non-pencil creation** use; the 14-case bake-off is re-runnable for a FLUX/new-model re-test). **No separate FloNode live smoke spent** — nb2 + nb_pro fired live in this bake-off via the same `invoke_image_edit` transport FloNode dispatches, so the wired routes are live-proven (Flo-A's deferral closed).
- **Ticket filed** (code-brain manual lane): **self-hosted FLUX + Shakker sketch-LoRA for pencil in-betweens** — the $0-ongoing future (control grain at generation time vs hoping an API preserves it); re-evaluate via this bake-off harness. Until then NB2/NB Pro own in-betweens.

## 2026-06-10 — Flo, Session A: the $0 Phase 5 generation-router skeleton (`generation.routing:` + `FloNode` + Maya cost-preview)

**What & why.** Built **Flo**, the Phase 5 generation router, as a $0 stub-green skeleton. Until now every frame generated through one model (NB2) at a flat $0.067 — [`pipeline/nodes/frame_generate.py`](pipeline/nodes/frame_generate.py) wraps the legacy `generate_frame()`, single-model. Flo makes generation **cost-routed + quality-tiered**: hero keyframes → NB Pro, standard → NB2, in-between/edit tiers declared as honest not-wired seams, and feeds Maya an accurate Phase-0 cost preview. The in-between transports stay declared seams for **Flo-B** (the costed fal.ai pencil-preservation pilot). Plan of record: [`docs/2026-06-10-flo-router-build-plan.md`](docs/2026-06-10-flo-router-build-plan.md) (scope LOCKED); kickoff: [`docs/2026-06-10-flo-router-session-a-kickoff.md`](docs/2026-06-10-flo-router-session-a-kickoff.md). Executed under [`docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md`](docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md): isolated worktree off `origin/main` `ac95869` (#42), `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` absent (no spend — stub-green throughout), divergence `0 0` before/after.

- **`generation.routing:` manifest block** in [`manifest.yaml`](manifest.yaml), additive under `generation:` (single-model fields kept for back-compat), mirroring [`docs/Image-Model-DR-2026/SYNTHESIS.md`](docs/Image-Model-DR-2026/SYNTHESIS.md) §2. Each route = `{transport, model, usd_per_frame, tier, status}`: `hero_keyframe` (nb_pro, $0.15, pro, **wired**), `standard_keyframe` (nb2 `gemini-3.1-flash-image-preview`, $0.07, draft, **wired**), `in_between_cheap` (fal_seedream, $0.02, **declared**), `in_between_mid` (fal_qwen, $0.021, **declared**), `mask_edit` (gpt_image_2, $0.21, **deferred**), `fallback: nb2`. **Cosmetic-honest (the T2/T3 lesson):** `status: declared/deferred` = config exists, transport NOT wired → Flo raises a clear `RouteNotWiredError`, never a silent mis-generation.
- **The router (TDD).** New [`pipeline/agents/frame_router.py`](pipeline/agents/frame_router.py): `resolve_route(shot, manifest, character) -> Route | None` maps `{shot_type (explicit on the frame spec, default standard_keyframe), tier, style_register}` → a `Route(transport, model, usd_per_frame, tier, status, shot_type, style_register)`. **Draft→pro escalation** (build-plan A2 "standard→hero"): a `standard_keyframe` resolved at `tier=pro` escalates to the `hero_keyframe` route; at draft it stays standard. No `routing:` block → returns `None` (the back-compat signal). `FloNode` (`@register_node("flo")`, AgentSpec) dispatches the resolved route — `nb_pro` → `invoke_image_edit` ([`nb_pro_runner.py`](pipeline/agents/nb_pro_runner.py)), `nb2` → the legacy `generate_frame()` path **unchanged**, `fal_*`/`gpt_image_2` → `RouteNotWiredError`. **Back-compat preserved:** no routing block → legacy single-model fall-through (pencil-test runs unaffected). The route taken is recorded in `AgentResult.notes` (museum credit + cost provenance). Registered via [`pipeline/nodes/__init__.py`](pipeline/nodes/__init__.py). Signatures verified against the real runner functions before dispatch (the "verify the transport, not the docstring" doctrine).
- **Maya cost-preview (TDD).** Extended `cost_estimator._phase_5_cost` ([`pipeline/agents/cost_estimator.py`](pipeline/agents/cost_estimator.py)) to sum the **full** routing table — declared/deferred in-between + mask-edit counts (`phases.phase_5.frame_count_<shot_type>`) price at their config estimate with a widened high band, and any budgeted not-wired route flips a new `confidence: "lowered"` flag (wired-only plans stay `"full"`). The wired hero/standard escalation-ladder math is preserved byte-for-byte; the `{low_usd, median_usd, high_usd}` return shape is unchanged (the additive `confidence` key is ignored by the band-sum).
- **Tests + green.** New [`tests/test_frame_router.py`](tests/test_frame_router.py) (15: resolution by shot_type + style_register, hero→nb_pro / standard→nb2, draft→pro escalation, declared→`RouteNotWiredError`, back-compat fall-through, AgentSpec conformance, cost pricing) + 2 new cost-estimator cases (full-table sum, declared-route lowered confidence). nb_pro exercises `invoke_image_edit`'s stub fallback (CI-green, no key); nb2 + fall-through monkeypatch the `generate_frame` subprocess boundary. Full contract suite [`tests/`](tests/) **483 passed** (1 pre-existing `google.genai` deprecation warning); seedance suite [`pipeline/tests/`](pipeline/tests/) **10 passed**. **Em's verdict baseline `traces/g6.1b-criteria-attached-2026-06-08.md` (`md5 2af75906502f1caf8857e18828ceb2e4`) byte-identical before and after** — Flo is purely additive; no `evals/vision_critic/` artifact touched.
- **Out of scope / not done (Flo-B):** the fal.ai Seedream/Qwen transports, the pencil-preservation benchmark, wiring any `in_between_*` route, the CLAUDE.md "Flo built" row flip (deferred until a live keyframe smoke confirms NB Pro/NB2 route live). No `declared` transport was wired this session.

Wired into [`scripts/build_museum.py`](scripts/build_museum.py) as `--t3-gate` (+ `--t3-limit/--t3-project/--t3-run-dir`), running **between** `--narrate` and `--render`. +7 tests [`tests/test_museum_t3_gate.py`](tests/test_museum_t3_gate.py) (pass→no-block, fail→block, patch `proposed_by`, contained-error→partial, all-errored→block, limit, live-vs-stub surfaced). **Do NOT touch `post_animatic`** — Phase 4 doesn't exist; placement-locked + ticketed.

## 2026-06-10 — T3 council, Session A: CLI smoke + Codie's Codex transport + the council engine ($0, stub-green)

**What & why.** Built the **engine half** of anima's last unbuilt critic tier — the T3 multi-CLI variance council (three heterogeneous peers → a distinct Opus chairman, Pattern C). $0: a subscription-absorbed CLI smoke test plus a stub-green build; no API-key billing. Session B (separate) wires the `pre_museum` gate, adds the `critics.t3:` config block, and runs the live smoke + Sage-tier bake-off. Plan of record: [`docs/2026-06-10-t3-council-build-plan.md`](docs/2026-06-10-t3-council-build-plan.md); kickoff: [`docs/2026-06-10-t3-council-session-a-kickoff.md`](docs/2026-06-10-t3-council-session-a-kickoff.md). Executed under [`docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md`](docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md): isolated worktree off `origin/main` `b2a06f2` (#40), `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` absent, divergence `0 0` before/after.

- **Step 0 smoke — Open-Q4 resolved against the real binaries** ([`docs/research/2026-06-10-t3-cli-multimodal-smoke.md`](docs/research/2026-06-10-t3-cli-multimodal-smoke.md), verbatim captures). **`agy` v1.0.4 REJECTS `-m`** (`flags provided but not defined: -m`, exit 2 — there is no model flag on `agy` at all), confirming the Anti-Gravity findings and **falsifying the `cli_runners.py` A2 docstring** that claims `-m gemini-3.1-pro` pins the model. **Reserved Decision 2 → Annie routes through the Gemini API** (`run_gemini_api_with_image`, `gemini-3.5-flash` pinned + `model_version` read-back), consistent with Em — *not* `agy` (also because `agy -p` is an agentic harness, not a clean vision call: it ran ~30 tool steps before viewing the test image). **Latent bug surfaced for Sean** (out of scope, not touched): `run_antigravity_with_image` builds `cmd = [agy, …, "-m", model, …]`, so a real agy call would fail exit-2 on the installed binary — uncaught because Em's prod transport is the Gemini API. `codex` is **not installed** here, so its live image invocation is unverified (Session B confirms); the documented shape is `codex exec --sandbox read-only --skip-git-repo-check` from `$HOME`. Video → **contact-sheet** path (`pipeline/contact_sheet.py`) confirmed; motion-proper blind spot accepted.
- **Codie's Codex transport (TDD).** New `run_codex_with_image` in [`pipeline/agents/cli_runners.py`](pipeline/agents/cli_runners.py): async subprocess mirroring `run_antigravity_with_image`, deterministic stub when the binary is absent (CI-green on a fresh machine), `RateCapExhausted` on empty-stdout-exit-0 or a quota signal (the honesty contract — never a silent verdict), returns `CLIResponse(cli="codex")`. `model` is **optional** (codex selects from `~/.codex/config.toml`; no silent-backend trap to guard, unlike agy). +7 tests in [`tests/test_cli_runners.py`](tests/test_cli_runners.py) (stub envelope, empty-images, success, empty-stdout→ratecap, stderr-quota→ratecap, timeout→124, `.ok`).
- **The council engine (TDD, the substantive build).** New [`pipeline/agents/t3_council.py`](pipeline/agents/t3_council.py) — `T3CouncilNode`, `@register_node("t3_council")`, satisfies `AgentSpec`. Parallel `asyncio.gather` fan-out of three peers — **Codie** (production/Codex) · **Annie** (visual+identity/Gemini API) · **Sage** (narrative/Opus SDK `invoke_opus_vision`) — each wrapped so **a peer erroring is a contained errored gap, never a run-abort** (the Gate-3 v1 lesson). Per-peer status promotion + council aggregate (`ok` / `partial` / `success-empty` / `error`; both-CLIs-capped → `partial`, mirroring code-brain `vault_critic.py`). A **separate** `invoke_opus_text` **chairman** (NOT a promoted peer) synthesizes the three reads → consensus + dissent + adjudication note + the council's recommended patches. Every peer + chairman emits `Patch(proposed_by="codie"|"annie"|"sage"|"chairman")`; the existing `stage_patches_hook` stages them (no new stager). Video artifacts reduce to a contact sheet. +10 tests in [`tests/test_t3_council.py`](tests/test_t3_council.py) (AgentSpec conformance, full-stub green, fan-out runs all three, **chairman is a separate call whose prompt carries the peer reads**, both-CLIs-capped→partial, all-errored→error-no-raise, contained-error, patch `proposed_by`, agreement score). Structural reference (`vault_critic.py`) provided fan-out + status only — the chairman is net-new.
- **Four standing-context preambles** mirroring `em-vision-critic-context.md`: [`codie`](pipeline/agents/prompts/codie-context.md) / [`annie`](pipeline/agents/prompts/annie-context.md) / [`sage`](pipeline/agents/prompts/sage-context.md) / [`chairman`](pipeline/agents/prompts/chairman-context.md)-context.md. ## 2026-06-10 — Tier 1 Em eval-suite close-out: Gate-2 golden-agreement judge CALIBRATED (~$1.50 costed) + merge-debris housekeeping

**What & why.** With all three of Em's axes now *measured* (verdict 0.97/1.00/0.00, citation 0.97, constructive fix-rate 0.667 #39), the suite needed to become **usable going forward** — the constructive axis costs ~$7.80/run, too dear to track between iterations. The cheap **Gate-2 golden-agreement proxy** ([`evals/vision_critic/diff_eval.py`](evals/vision_critic/diff_eval.py): *does Em's proposed clause express the SAME fix as Sean's ratified golden?*) was **built but uncalibrated** — and an uncalibrated judge "launders a guess into a verdict." This run calibrates it against a Sean-labeled sample so fix-rate can be tracked for pennies between costed runs. Executed under [`docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md`](docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md) (isolated worktree off `origin/main` `1c4cd9e`, subscription billing for the Opus judge with `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` absent, `GEMINI_API_KEY` bounded from `.env` for capture only). Field report: [`docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-10-em-gate2-judge-calibration.md`](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-10-em-gate2-judge-calibration.md); trace: [`evals/vision_critic/traces/gate2-calibration-2026-06-10.md`](evals/vision_critic/traces/gate2-calibration-2026-06-10.md). Kickoff: [`docs/2026-06-08-tier1-eval-suite-closeout-kickoff.md`](docs/2026-06-08-tier1-eval-suite-closeout-kickoff.md).

- **Calibration harness (TDD, scaffold-first per SF03 discipline).** New [`evals/vision_critic/calibrate_diff_judge.py`](evals/vision_critic/calibrate_diff_judge.py) + [`tests/test_calibrate_diff_judge.py`](tests/test_calibrate_diff_judge.py) (22 tests). Built fresh because nothing existed: **N=5 majority vote** over `score_golden_agreement` (sampling consistency > verbalized confidence, handbook §3.5); a **match-class** confusion matrix where positive=match, so **FPR = FP/(FP+TN)** is the *dangerous over-call* rate — deliberately distinct from `scoring.py`'s verdict-suite `false_pass_rate = FN/(TP+FN)`; **Cohen's κ** (no helper in `scoring.py`); the `match=None` "no diff proposed" contract preserved (excluded from the matrix, never a 0); a credential-free `--check-only` synthetic pipeline; subprocess-isolated + per-case-contained live capture (each case `score.py --only … --dump-patches` in a fresh interpreter — dodges the exit-144 teardown race a 30-case in-process Em+Opus loop would hit); and the calibration-set + labeling-sheet builders.
- **Costed capture (~$1.50 Gemini + subscription Opus).** Em run LIVE on the 30 `identity_style` defect cases → [`evals/vision_critic/calibration/em_diffs_2026-06-09.jsonl`](evals/vision_critic/calibration/em_diffs_2026-06-09.jsonl): **30/30 cases, 29 non-empty, 0 errored, 0 STUB** (`anatomy-ad3` proposed no diff → `match=None`). Both transports proof-verified real (not stubbed) before the full run.
- **Balanced 54-pair set + Sean labels.** 30 real (Em-clause vs own golden) + 18 cross-class negatives + 6 **hand-authored** hard same-class negatives (within-class goldens are near-identical, so same-class case pairings would mostly *match* — hard negatives can't be auto-generated). Sean labeled 53 (1 null), balance **23 match / 30 no-match**. The judge is blind to pair `kind`.
- **Result — PASS on iteration 1.** Opus judge N=5 vs Sean: **κ 0.885 / FPR 0.067 / precision 0.917 / recall 0.957**, clears the **κ ≥ 0.6 AND FPR ≤ 0.10** bar (Sean's call). 4/6 classes perfect (κ 1.00, FPR 0.00). **Both FPs are palette** — the judge under-weights *completeness* (a partial fix, e.g. hair-recolored-but-stubble-ignored, read as a match); named as the residual + re-open condition. **view-correctness FPR 0.00** — the judge safely rejects Em's wrong-target-view fixes, independently corroborating Gate-3's finding that view is Em's weakest constructive axis. No prompt iteration (bar met; chasing 2 subtle palette FPs on 53 pairs would overfit). **Verdict: the proxy is trustworthy to track fix-rate between costed Gate-3 runs.** Corpus + raw payload committed under [`evals/vision_critic/calibration/`](evals/vision_critic/calibration/).
- **Housekeeping (Part B).** **B2:** archived 5 executed/superseded Gate-3 docs to `docs/COMPLETED/` (stage-2 handoff, ratification plan, eval-suite-completion-kickoff, prompt-diff-eval-design) and `docs/OLD/` (gate3-costed-handoff), fixed inbound links in active docs only (verified no danglers). **B1:** deleted the stale local branch; the 7 stale *remote* branches were already gone on GitHub (auto-deleted on PR merge — verified via PR state #28/#34–#39, since `git branch -r --merged` structurally can't see squash merges), stale local tracking refs pruned.
- **Green + guard.** `tests/test_calibrate_diff_judge.py` 22 passed; full contract suite **432 passed**; seedance suite 10 passed. Verdict baseline `traces/g6.1b-criteria-attached-2026-06-08.md` (`md5 2af75906502f1caf8857e18828ceb2e4`) **byte-identical before and after** — calibration is additive (a new ruler over Em's *diffs*, never a re-score of her verdicts). CLAUDE.md Em row + the completion-plan inventory updated. **The Em eval suite is now complete: all three axes measured AND the cheap proxy calibrated.**

## 2026-06-08 — G6.9 Gate-3 (Stage 2): Em's constructive axis MEASURED + per-case containment fix (~$7.85 costed)

**What & why.** Ran the **one costed Gate-3 baseline** that closes Em's third axis — does applying her proposed corrective clause actually clear the defect with identity held? Verdict (0.97/1.00/0.00) and citation (cites-correct 0.97) were already measured; this is the fix-rate. Executed the [Stage 2 runbook](docs/2026-06-08-em-g6.9-gate3-stage2-fleet-ops-handoff.md) under [`docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md`](docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md): isolated worktree off `origin/main` `c01920c` (#38), subscription billing (`ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` absent, no `--allow-api-key`), single owner, `.env` copied in, divergence checked before/after. Field report: [`docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-08-em-g6.9-gate3-fixrate.md`](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-08-em-g6.9-gate3-fixrate.md); trace: [`evals/vision_critic/traces/gate3-fixrate-2026-06-08.md`](evals/vision_critic/traces/gate3-fixrate-2026-06-08.md).

- **Result (`both+null 12×3`, LIVE; 12/12 cases, 0 errored gaps, wall 2.45 hr, ~$7.80):** **overall normalized lift `(em−null)/(golden−null)` = 0.667** (em 0.33 / golden 0.44 / null 0.11; proposal-rate **1.00**) — Em's fixes recover ~⅔ of the golden's lift over the placebo floor, **discriminative on all six classes**. Per class: em ≥ golden on anatomy-count (+2.0) / shading-register (+2.0) / proportion (+1.0); below-golden-above-placebo on palette (+0.5) / construction-lines (+0.33); **view-correctness 0.00** (Em's declared-view clauses cleared 0/6 on the no-regen path vs golden 3/6 — the next constructive-axis target). **Small-N first read** (6 outcomes/class/arm, stderr≈0.33 — directional, not precise; the `+2.0`s ride on small golden−null denominators); the fuller **30×5** stays deferred.
- **Harness fix (TDD, the reason this is a code change not just a run).** The v1 launch **crashed on case #0** (`anatomy-ad1-six-fingers`, identity_critical) after an uncaught `subprocess.TimeoutExpired` at the 900s `_PER_CASE_TIMEOUT_S` — it propagated out of the orchestrator loop and **aborted the whole run with 0 cases recorded**. The runbook's §0 claim that the live path treats a failed worker as "an honest errored gap, not a silent zero" was **false against the tree**: Stage 1 (#37) isolated only the *worker*; the orchestrator loop ([patch_efficacy.py:617](evals/vision_critic/patch_efficacy.py)) had no try/except. Fix: extracted **`_run_live_cases`** — a per-case `try/except` that records a timeout/worker-failure as an honest errored gap `(name, reason)` and **continues** (mirrors `score.py`'s containment), surfacing an `errored: [...]` list in the output JSON. RED→GREEN via [`tests/test_patch_efficacy_containment.py`](tests/test_patch_efficacy_containment.py) (timeout-as-gap, RuntimeError-as-gap, all-errored→empty-effs+N/A-lift-no-crash); stale `COSTED-RUN HARDENING NOTE` docstring corrected.
- **Timeout, diagnosed not guessed.** A $0 code scan + a bounded ~$0.24 probe (one identity_critical case at `--rerolls 1` = **501s**) showed it was **slow, not hung**: each model call is `asyncio.wait_for`-bounded at 120s (sdk_runners.py:116), but `identity_critical` forces Opus escalation on every re-critique (~104s/call, near the ceiling) → ~1288s per case at rerolls=3, over the 900s cap. `_PER_CASE_TIMEOUT_S` raised 900 → **1800s** (data-justified comment; the containment fix is the backstop for any straggler). The re-run then completed with **0 gaps** at 1800s.
- **Green + guard.** Full contract suite **410 passed** (1 pre-existing unrelated `google.genai` deprecation warning) after the fix. Verdict baseline `traces/g6.1b-criteria-attached-2026-06-08.md` (`md5 2af75906502f1caf8857e18828ceb2e4`) **byte-identical before and after** — G6.9 is additive, never a re-score of the verdict baseline. CLAUDE.md Em row updated with the fix-rate (its first constructive-axis number).

## 2026-06-08 — G6.9 Gate-3 Stage 1: subprocess-per-case isolation for the patch-efficacy loop ($0, no spend)

**What & why.** The $0 wiring step the costed Gate-3 fix-rate baseline is gated behind (Stage 1 of [`docs/2026-06-08-em-eval-suite-completion-plan.md`](docs/2026-06-08-em-eval-suite-completion-plan.md)). Before this, `patch_efficacy.py`'s live loop ran every case **in-process** — but the live re-critique spawns Em's async Opus children, so a single-process run risks the **exit-144 interpreter-teardown race** that made the 2026-06-07 attempt "measure nothing." Now each LIVE case runs in a **fresh worker** that emits its `CaseEfficacy` as a stdout sentinel; the orchestrator parses it. Mirrors `score.py`'s `_run_case_subprocess` pattern (the orchestrator is the side isolated from the teardown signal, never the worker — detaching the worker breaks Claude Code auth for the Opus-SDK child, verified 2026-06-02).

- **New in [`evals/vision_critic/patch_efficacy.py`](evals/vision_critic/patch_efficacy.py):** `--only <case>` worker mode (`_run_worker`) runs one case's arm loop and prints `EFFICACY_JSON:<asdict>` flushed-before-return; `_run_case_subprocess` (the parent) spawns `python -m evals.vision_critic.patch_efficacy --only … --arm … --rerolls …`, reads the sentinel from stdout first (a worker that flushed then crashed at teardown is still captured; one that died before emitting is an honest `RuntimeError`), **no `start_new_session`**; `_efficacy_from_dict` rebuilds the nested dataclass so the parent gets real `ArmResult`/`RerollOutcome` (clear_rate/band) objects. Shared `_build_runners` / `_em_kwargs` de-duplicate runner setup. `main()` now routes the **LIVE** path through one subprocess per case; the **`--stub`** path stays **in-process** (fakes spawn no async children — fast, CI-safe).
- **TDD, $0.** Two new tests in [`tests/test_patch_efficacy_harness.py`](tests/test_patch_efficacy_harness.py): a stub round-trip that asserts the worker's `CaseEfficacy` is byte-identical (`asdict` deep-equal) to the in-process run (the sentinel handshake), and an honest-error case (unknown case → no sentinel → `RuntimeError`). Verified green: **15** harness tests, **407** contract tests (`tests/`), eval runner 58 passed (+6 pre-existing motion `xpassed`); `--stub` → `PREFLIGHT OK $7.80` (nb2=90 em=120) + valid `normalized_lift` JSON; `--check-only` exits 0; `--only` worker emits exactly one sentinel. **No model spend; the verdict baseline `traces/g6.1b-criteria-attached-2026-06-08.md` is untouched** (this is the second axis of the ruler, not a re-score of the first).
- **Next (Stage 2, costed, fleet-ops):** `--check-only` → live `--dump-patches` capture-proof → the ~$7.80 `both+null 12×3` run → trace + field report → CLAUDE.md Em-row fix-rate.

## 2026-06-08 — G6.9 Step 3 setup: null/placebo arm + normalized lift + em-capture ($0; costed run staged)

**What & why.** $0 machinery so the Gate 3 empirical baseline is turnkey when greenlit (no spend here). Implements Sean's locked attribution decision (2026-06-08 follow-on plan, decision #3): the clean-pair apply mechanism has a per-class FLOOR — a useless clause can still regenerate a clean frame — so raw fix-rate over-credits Em. The fix is a measured floor + a floor-corrected headline. Runbook: [`docs/2026-06-08-g6.9-gate3-costed-handoff.md`](docs/2026-06-08-g6.9-gate3-costed-handoff.md).

- **Null/placebo arm** (`evals/vision_critic/patch_efficacy.py`) — `--arm` gains `null` / `both+null` / `all`; **`both+null` is the new default** and the locked first-run config. The null arm splices a fixed defect-orthogonal placebo (`_NULL_CLAUSE = "with a calm, evenly-lit, neutral background"`) through the same clean-pair mechanism as em/golden, measuring how often the base clears **regardless** of corrective content.
- **Normalized lift** — `normalized_lift(agg)` reports, per class + overall, raw em/golden/null clear-rates + `lift = (em − null)/(golden − null)` + a `discriminative` flag. `golden ≈ null` ⇒ `lift: null, discriminative: false` — the instrument has no power on that class (a finding, not a guess). 1.0 = em matches the golden's lift over the floor; 0.0 = no better than placebo; <0 = worse.
- **Live em-capture** — `_capture_em_value` runs Em LIVE on the defect fixture (the Gate 0 capture path) to get her actual `proposed_patches[].value` for the em arm (one call/case; None when Em proposed nothing → the arm records `skipped_no_proposal`, never a 0). Replaces the deferred `_live_em_value` stub.
- **Cost estimate** updated for the em-arm capture (one Em call/case) + the third arm: **first run `both+null --sample 12 --rerolls 3` ≈ $7.80** (nb2=90, em=120 incl. 12 captures); printed before any spend.
- **Tests** — `tests/test_gate3_null_lift.py` (9): null-arm splice, three-arm independence, lift math (floor-cancel, no-power, N/A-without-all-arms), em-capture (returns clause / None on no-patch), cost-with-capture. Full `tests/` **405 passed**; verdict baseline byte-identical (`md5 2af75906…`). **Still no costed run** — `patch_efficacy --check-only` refuses live until #34's ratified goldens land; the handoff doc gates the spend.
