## 2026-06-08 — G6.9 diff-eval: $0 infrastructure built (the second axis of Em's ruler) — costed runs DEFERRED

**What & why.** After G5/G6.1b the eval suite measures Em's *verdicts* (0.97/1.00/0.00) and *citations* (0.97) but **nothing** about her *constructive* output — the `proposed_patches` (prompt diffs) she stages. The Critic Stack contract is "T2 **proposes prompt diffs**, not pass/fail"; "flags correctly" and "proposes a fix that helps" can diverge arbitrarily. G6.9 builds the second scoring axis. Executes [`docs/2026-06-08-g6.9-prompt-diff-eval-handoff.md`](docs/2026-06-08-g6.9-prompt-diff-eval-handoff.md). Sean-scoped this push to **all $0 infrastructure, stub-tested green, no costed run** (goldens drafted-for-ratification; the costed Gate 2 calibration + Gate 3 baseline are a deferred follow-on behind ratification + a spend go-ahead). **The ratified verdict baseline is purely additive-protected:** `evals/vision_critic/traces/g6.1b-criteria-attached-2026-06-08.md` stays byte-identical (`md5 2af75906502f1caf8857e18828ceb2e4`, verified before+after).

- **Gate 0 — diffs are now captured (they were silently dropped).** `CaseScore` gains `proposed_patches: list[dict]` (plain dicts, never the frozen `Patch`, so the `asdict`↔`CaseScore(**…)` subprocess round-trip survives); `score.py::_score_one` threads `result.proposed_patches`, `consensus_scores` carries them from the verdict-winning run (like cites), `render_per_case_detail` renders a sibling "Proposed diffs" block (never inside the cite table), and both stub paths (`_force_stub_runners`, `conftest.make_vision_verdict`) + the CI `runner.py` construction now stage a representative diff on flagged verdicts so capture is exercised. New `score.py --dump-patches` (+ `--only --stub`) is the **$0 §0 pre-flight** — prints the captured diffs and asserts non-empty for a defect case before any model call (the 2026-06-07 "flag silently off → measured nothing" failure mode dies here). Pure `scoring.diff_cite_precision_recall` adds precision **AND** recall on diff cites (distinct from the recall-only verdict scorer; locked #4).
- **Gate 1 — draft golden corpus (Sean ratifies).** All 30 `identity_style` defect cases in `cases.yaml` gain `golden_diff` (a bare corrective clause — the inverse of the defect) + `golden_diff_ratified: false`. I drafted; Sean ratifies/edits at review. Inserted by pure-text edit (88 YAML comments preserved; pyyaml round-trip would have destroyed them; ruamel unavailable). View-correctness goldens are declared-view corrections (label-side). **No costed run may proceed while any sampled golden is unratified** (Gate 3 §0 refuses).
- **Gate 2 + Gate 4 — judge-based scorers (`evals/vision_critic/diff_eval.py`).** Gate 2 golden-agreement (judge says Em's clause expresses the same fix as the golden, binary) + diff cite precision/recall, segmented per defect-class. Gate 4 triage rubric (targets-defect / actionable / no-character-re-description (Seedance) / style-neutral), explicitly **never the headline** (judge-on-judge). Judges are **pluggable** (default Gate 2→opus-text, Gate 4→gemini-flash; wired but NOT invoked this push); calibration is mandatory and deferred. `--check-only` runs the whole pipeline over all 30 cases on a **stub judge, $0**.
- **Gate 3 — empirical loop machinery (`patch_efficacy.py` + pure `prompt_apply.py`), NO live run.** `prompt_apply` parses the fixture-corpus md and **deterministically splices** a corrective clause onto the defect case's **clean PAIR** prompt (no LLM "apply" step; robust to the corpus's three defect grammars; always re-emits the full canonical style line so palette/shading corrections can't ship axis-deficient). `patch_efficacy` runs the dual-arm loop (golden = positive control, em = under test), per re-roll scoring **defect cleared AND identity held** (cite-based: original defect cite gone, no new drift cite), N re-rolls → clear-rate band, view-correctness on a no-regeneration branch. Guards baked in: per-re-roll `reject_reason` defeats the content-addressed cache (N re-rolls stay independent), `stub_fallback` in a live run is a hard error, "Em proposed nothing" is a separate measured outcome (proposal-rate vs fix-rate-given-proposed, never a 0). **§0 `--check-only`** asserts wiring ($0); a **live run is refused** until goldens are ratified, `GEMINI_API_KEY` is present, and `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is unset. Cost estimate printed before any loop.
- **Apply-mechanism + attribution caveat (documented, deferred to the costed phase — a Sean-decision on real Em patch semantics):** the clean-pair base means a *useless* corrective clause can still regenerate a clean frame, inflating fix-rate; the golden positive-control arm + the identity-held re-critique keep the signal honest, and the first costed run refines the rule against real captured diffs. Also deferred: judge calibration, wiring the live em-arm to a `score.py` patch-capture run, and wrapping the costed re-critique in `score.py`'s subprocess-per-case isolation (the in-process path is safe for stubs but inherits Em's async-teardown race live).
- **Tests (all credential-free, additive):** `tests/test_gate0_patch_capture.py` (9), `tests/test_patch_efficacy_apply.py` (9), `tests/test_gate2_diff_score.py` (7), `tests/test_patch_efficacy_harness.py` (13). Full `tests/` suite **350 passed**; `evals/vision_critic/runner.py` 58 passed / 6 xpassed (pre-existing motion xpass); `pipeline/tests/` 10 passed. **No CLAUDE.md Em-row update** — per the handoff, that waits for a real measured fix-rate number, which this push does not produce.

## 2026-06-08 — SF03 proportion gate (G6.4): probe RAN → Approach A built + retroactively verified

**What & why.** Follows the scaffold entry below. The costed make-or-break probe ran, Sean chose Approach A, the Approach-A feeder + measurement hardening shipped, and the gate was retroactively run against the locked sean-anchor turnarounds (the A4 loop close). Field report: [`docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-08-sf03-probe-and-build.md`](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-08-sf03-probe-and-build.md).

- **Probe verdict (4 NB2 Flash plates, ~sub-$0.20):** NB2 **honors the heads-tall armature** — front/profile/back seated crown-to-feet and auto-measured **7.05–7.15 heads** (inside [6.5,7.5]); view-invariance held. The lone ¾ "fail" (8.29) was NB2 redrawing the grid with **9 lines instead of 8** (a ruler-rescale), not a figure-proportion miss. Plates committed: [`docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-08-sf03-probe-plates/`](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-08-sf03-probe-plates/).
- **Approach A built** (Sean's call): `measure_proportion` armature branch **hardened** to anchor on the bold crown/feet lines + the **known division count** (`armature_divisions` or `round(target)`), not the detected line count — the ¾ case re-derives to ~7.25 → pass, and grid line-count drift is surfaced in the verdict detail. Added `build_armature_underlay()` (the canonical 1:N ladder) + `emit_gridded_model_sheet()` (the constrained-generation feeder writing `turnarounds/armature/<name>.png`) + `ProportionSpec.armature_divisions`.
- **Key finding — Approach A is PREVENTION, not retroactive AUDIT.** The probe drew a full-body 7-heads figure from a *head-only* anchor + armature, i.e. **NB2 fits the figure TO the grid**. So re-gridding an existing clean plate restretches it and *hides* drift. Sound Approach A = generate body turnarounds against the armature from the start (born 1:7; the gate confirms NB2 obeyed). A naive "regrid the finished plate" auto-step would be unsound, so it is **not** wired into Cy's hot loop; with no current consumer (sean locked, mascot opt-out), the Cy auto-wiring is a documented follow-on. The primitives + the probe are the reference implementation.
- **Retroactive verification (A4 loop close):** ran the gate on the already-locked `characters/sean-anchor/turnarounds/body-*.png` (the 1:7 re-lock from `b7323e3`, human-gated). All five → **`indeterminate [extent_only]`** → blocked. Persisted: [`docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-08-sf03-retroactive-sean-anchor.json`](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-08-sf03-retroactive-sean-anchor.json). **This is a surfaced finding, not a fix:** the gate cannot SF03-certify plates that predate constrained generation — *not* evidence they're off-proportion (the human gate judged them 1:7), just that the automated gate can't *confirm* it retroactively. Certifying deterministically requires re-baking the five through the Approach-A feeder (its own decided work).
- **Tests:** +4 (hardened measure, divisions override, armature generator, emit feeder). **Full contract suite 358 green, 0 regressions.** Commits `8a392da` (scaffold) · `9d95cf5` (probe) · `476d9e6` (Approach-A primitives).

## 2026-06-08 — SF03 proportion gate (G6.4): scaffold built CI-green (probe + feeder pending)

**What & why.** SF03 ("proportion drift") is a QA gate anima declared but never automated — the cost was concrete: sean-anchor's body turnarounds baked into a **locked** Bible at ~1:4–1:5.3 heads-tall against a 1:7 target, and nothing caught it (the only proportion-adjacent signal, Cy's Pass-2.5 similarity gate, is record-only and measures *identity*, not *geometry*). Two prior spikes proved you can't reliably *recover* head-to-body ratio from finished stylized art (DINOv2 NO-GO; chin-detection NO-GO). This build executes the parked design ([`docs/2026-06-03-sf03-proportion-gate-design.md`](docs/2026-06-03-sf03-proportion-gate-design.md)) under the [SF03 build handoff](docs/2026-06-04-sf03-proportion-gate-build-handoff.md): don't reverse-engineer proportion — **constrain** against a known vertical armature, then **verify** the render against it (head-to-body ratio is vertical + view-invariant).

**Build order = scaffold-first** (Sean's 2026-06-08 planning call): the measurement is deterministic PIL/numpy, so the whole gate + hard-lock wiring + tests + retroactive checker were built and verified CI-green **before** any costed probe. The gate ships in an honest `indeterminate-until-fed` state; the pending NB2 probe only decides which *input-feeder* to wire (Approach A gridded sheets vs Approach B stored landmarks).

- **New module** [`pipeline/agents/proportion_gate.py`](pipeline/agents/proportion_gate.py) — per-character `ProportionSpec` (declared / opt_out / undeclared), the reliable vertical primitives (`figure_extent` = crown/feet of the ink mask; `detect_armature_lines` = full-width printed rules), and `measure_proportion` with three modes feeding **one** verdict shape: **A** armature grid-alignment, **B** stored landmarks, **extent_only** fallback → `indeterminate` (never a faked pass). Never raises (mirrors `similarity_gate`).
- **Per-character spec, never hardcoded 1:7** — sean-anchor's `character.yaml` gains `head_to_body_target: 7.0` + `tolerance_heads: [6.5, 7.5]`; claude-mascot (box-creature) gets `proportions.sf03: opt_out`. Makes `IR.sean.proportion.head-to-body-1-to-7` *checkable*.
- **Cy wiring** — `plate_status_fields` runs on `turnarounds/body-*.png` inside `_run_plate` (after the Pass-2.5 score + the regen re-score), persisting `sf03_*` through `_persist_plate_verdicts` unchanged. Body-only; head/props/expressions/motion get `sf03_gate: skipped`.
- **HARD gate at lock** — `approve_bible` recomputes `gate_body_turnarounds` on the **committed** body turnarounds (not the ephemeral run trail — the committed pixels are what's being locked) and **refuses the lock (rc 1)** on any `fail`/`indeterminate`/`error`, plus the anti-silent-pass guard (undeclared spec + body plates present = BLOCK; `opt_out` is the only no-spec path to a lock). The already-locked early-return runs first, so the gate guards NEW locks only and can't retro-block an existing Bible.
- **Read-only retroactive verifier** — new `pipeline bible check-proportion --character-dir …` prints per-plate verdicts, rc 1 on block, never touches `locked`. Smoke-run on the real sean-anchor today returns all 5 body turnarounds `indeterminate [extent_only]` → the honest A4 finding (no armature/landmarks yet; the probe-chosen feeder fills this seam).
- **Tests** — `tests/test_proportion_gate.py` (32, synthetic cream/graphite PIL fixtures, no committed binaries, credential-free) + 1 Cy wiring guard + 10 bible-CLI gate/check-proportion tests. **Gate A green: contract suite 354 passed (was 312), seedance 10 passed, 0 regressions.**

**Pending (next):** the costed NB2 armature probe (does NB2 honor an armature underlay?) → STOP for Sean's A-vs-B call → wire the winning feeder → formal retroactive verification → CLAUDE.md SF03-row update + field report.

## 2026-06-07 — G6.1b Part A LANDED: criteria-text decoupled from reference-images (non-costed code); §0 gate + costed run pending

**What & why.** The [2026-06-07 re-baseline](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-07-em-g6.1-rebaseline.md) proved G6.1's steps 1/2/4 were **inert reference-blind**: the criteria block (the only path the authored handles reach Em) was gated behind `attach_references`, which is OFF in every shipped/G5/2026-06-07 config — so Em's prompt was byte-identical to G5 and only the scorer (step 3) moved. Part A of the [G6.1b handoff](docs/2026-06-07-em-g6.1b-criteria-text-decoupling-handoff.md) adds an **independent lever** to turn the criteria text ON without turning reference images ON (images carry the 2026-06-04 precision regression; the criteria text does not). This is the non-costed code change; the costed N=5 criteria-attached run is gated behind a $0 §0 pre-flight and held for Sean's greenlight (pause-after-§0, his call).

**`pipeline/agents/vision_critic.py`.** New `_attach_criteria_text(t2_cfg)` (mirrors `_attach_references`, default False). The `_build_prompt` criteria-block gate is now `if self._attach_criteria_text(t2_cfg) or self._attach_references(t2_cfg)` — attached when EITHER lever is set; the references-on path is unchanged (still attaches both images + criteria). **`run()`'s image bundle is untouched** — it stays gated on `_attach_references` alone, so `attach_criteria_text=True, attach_references=False` ⇒ criteria text present, **zero images** (`n_references == 0`, no "Reference plates" section). One reference-assuming sentence in `_criteria_block` reworded ("a rule the references confirm is honored" → "a rule the frame honors") for criteria-text-only mode; the sentinel and the copy-verbatim/no-HF-SF-substitution block are intact (they are the point).

**`evals/vision_critic/score.py`.** Mirrored the `--attach-references` plumbing for `--attach-criteria-text` (argparse → in-memory manifest mutation → `_run_case_subprocess` worker-cmd propagation → call site). `_refs_label` is now three-state — `references (images+criteria)` / `criteria-text (images off)` / `blind (attach_references off)` — and the attach-mode rides into the trace `model_label` header, so the persistent `.md` can **never read "blind" when criteria-text was on** (the prior run's invisible miss). New additive `--dump-prompt`: with `--only`, builds the prompt exactly as `run()` would (honoring both flags) and exits before any model call — the $0 §0 pre-flight that proves the criteria block reaches Em.

**Tests (credential-free, CI-green).** New `tests/test_score_attach_criteria_text.py` (engages-block label, default-blind, **worker-cmd propagation**, flag-independence). New anti-repeat coverage in `tests/test_vision_critic_criteria.py` — the test that would have caught the prior run: with `attach_criteria_text=True, attach_references=False` the built prompt **contains** the sentinel + a net-new `IR.sean.view.declared-view-matches-drawn` handle AND attaches **zero images** (no "Reference plates"); the both-off control attaches no block. `tests/` **312 passed**; `evals/vision_critic/runner.py` **58 passed / 6 xpassed** (verified byte-identical to clean f1bae9d — the xpass is a pre-existing stub-verdict artifact, not induced by this change).

**Held for ratification.** No baseline promotion, no CLAUDE.md Em-row edit, no merge to main. The repo manifest default stays `attach_criteria_text` absent (off); the lever is run-scoped only. Next: §0 dump → Sean greenlight → the single costed N=5 criteria-attached run (treatment vs the 2026-06-07 reference-blind control).

## 2026-06-07 — G6.1 re-baseline RAN (step 5, N=5 reference-blind) — PENDING Sean's ratification

**What & why.** Ran the single N=5 majority-vote re-baseline after steps 1–4 landed, config identical to G5 except the surface changes (reference-blind, gemini-3.5-flash pinned via `gemini_api`, opus-4.7 escalation, subprocess-per-case, `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` absent). 52 cases × 5 = 260 case-runs, 1 empty-cites invariant trip (motion-w1-arc, N=1 JSON parse, majority-recovered). **Scope correction discovered against the tree (load-bearing).** The Bible criteria block reaches Em **only** through `attach_references` ([`pipeline/agents/vision_critic.py:381`](pipeline/agents/vision_critic.py#L381); `ctx.criteria` is consumed nowhere else Em-facing). This run is **reference-blind**, so the criteria block is **off** and Em's prompt is **byte-identical to G5** — meaning **steps 1/2/4 (Bible rules, stylus reframe, criteria-block surfacing) are INERT for Em's behaviour here.** Only step 3 (the scorer) moves the number. The handoff's step-5 "expected outcomes" (*construction/shading by surfacing, view/anatomy now citeable*) **cannot occur reference-blind** — they need the criteria block attached. Run-blind-as-is was Sean's explicit call after this was surfaced (2026-06-07). So this is a **scorer + verdict re-confirm at 52 cases**, not a measurement of the Bible authoring's effect on Em.

**Results (performs n=46, vs ratified G5 performs 0.97/1.00/0.00, cites 0.03):**
- **Safety HELD:** recall **1.00**, false_pass **0.00** (band 0.00–0.03); all 30 single-axis performs defects caught (FN=0), motion 6/6 flagged.
- **Precision 0.97 → 0.94** — 2 clean FPs: `clean-c06` (known, unchanged orientation FP, stays red) and `clean-c01` (NEW: majority-borderline flip). **Attribution (precise, per the hard line):** NOT the 9 new rules over-triggering — those are **provably inert blind** (criteria block off; no edit touches clean-c01's prompt). It is **N=5 sampling variance on a marginal clean fixture** (clean-c01 flags soft construction lines + thin hatching + stylus-absence; the stylus-absence flag is exactly what step 2 fixes, but step 2 is blind-gated-off). Reported as 0.94, not tuned toward 0.97.
- **Citation axis 0.03 → 0.27** (full=6 / partial=5 / none=21 over 32 flagged). Source, per-class: **proportion 5/5 full** (matcher/clean naming), **view 4/5 partial** (all via HF03 — Em confabulates `IR.sean.view.*`, never cites the authored `declared-view-matches-drawn`), **anatomy 1/4 full** (ad1 string coincidence), **palette 1/6 partial** (pad6 SF02), **construction 5/5 none + shading 5/5 none** (all SF01/HF05 substitution; authored style handles never cited). The construction/shading/view-handle/palette-handle misses are exactly what surfacing (step 4) + authored rules (step 1) target — and can't fix blind. This run is the clean scorer-only control; a future criteria-attached run isolates steps 1/2/4.

**Policy note carried for post-hoc re-score (Sean's flag, no change this run).** view→HF03 partial is inconsistent with style being excluded now that view has a reachable handle — but blind, view behaves like construction/shading (confabulation), so the asymmetry is policy, not behaviour. Re-scorable for free from the persisted per-class table: symmetric-strict (drop view→HF03) → performs cites **0.20**; symmetric-lenient (add style→SF01/HF05) → **0.42**. Recommend deciding after a criteria-attached run.

**Held for ratification.** No CLAUDE.md Em-row / Critic Stack edit, no baseline promotion, no PR-to-main until Sean ratifies. Trace + field report committed to the branch as evidence (separate from the steps-1–4 surface checkpoint).

## 2026-06-07 — G6.1 surface changes LANDED (steps 1–4); re-baseline (step 5) pending Sean's greenlight

**What & why.** Executed the four non-costed surface changes of the G6.1 citation-grounding handoff ([`docs/2026-06-06-em-g6.1-citation-grounding-handoff.md`](docs/2026-06-06-em-g6.1-citation-grounding-handoff.md)) in an isolated worktree off `origin/main`. Pre-flight clean (`main…origin/main` = `0 0`); ratified baseline traces verified byte-identical (`ff0d4fe…`) before and after — **not re-scored**.

**Step 1 — geometry IR rules authored (sean-anchor Bible, `bible add`, audited).** Nine new rules appended to the locked Bible via the additive path (now 31 rules, schema `version` stays `1.2`, re-locked at `content_version 1.3.0`, audit trail in `runs/2026-06-07-em-g6.1-citation-grounding/bible_audit.jsonl`). Five `IR.sean.view.*` (declared-view-matches-drawn — the `clean-c06` resolver, with the screen-relative facing convention authored explicitly — plus three-quarter-both-eyes-visible / profile-far-eye-occluded / front-symmetry / back-no-face) and four `IR.sean.anatomy.*` (finger-count-five-per-hand / hand-count-two / limb-count-four / leg-count-two). Handles drawn from Em's own observed citation vocabulary (2026-06-04 mini-run Q3) so she copies rather than confabulates. **Prerequisite discovered against the tree:** `view` was **not** in `VALID_IR_CATEGORIES` ([`pipeline/criteria.py`](pipeline/criteria.py)) — `IR.sean.view.*` would fail validation. Added `view` to the closed IR vocab (ten→eleven categories; a deliberate expansion — view-correctness is already a first-class geometry class in the layer-ownership map), and updated the exact-set assertion in [`tests/test_criteria_ir_namespace.py`](tests/test_criteria_ir_namespace.py). Proportion needed no Bible change (the existing `IR.sean.proportion.head-to-body-1-to-7` is correct; its gap is the matcher, step 3).

**Step 2 — stylus rule scoped to conditional (`bible mutate`, audited).** Reframed `IR.sean.prop.stylus-right-hand-always` from absolute ("in every frame… omits the stylus entirely is a hard violation") to **conditional continuity**: WHEN a stylus is depicted it must be right-handed with the three-finger grip, but a frame where no stylus is depictable (portrait crop above the hands, clean turnaround, empty-handed by beat intent) is on-model without one and must not be flagged for its absence. This removes the 4 stylus-free clean-fixture false positives (c02/c03/c05/c13) the references re-test surfaced, and with step 1 completes both `attach_references` re-open preconditions.

**Step 3 — scorer: leaf-normalized matcher + split axes + tiered credit + clean-FP fix ([`evals/vision_critic/scoring.py`](evals/vision_critic/scoring.py)).** `cites_correctness` now returns a graded `float | None` (was `bool | None`): **full (1.0)** for a leaf-normalized IR-handle match, **partial (0.5)** for the correct manifest QA reason-code keyed to the expected defect class (proportion→SF03, view→HF03, pose→HF04, identity face/hair→SF02; anatomy/style intentionally have none — they must cite the real handle now), else **none (0.0)**. New `normalize_cite` canonicalizes namespace (`sean-anchor`→`sean`) and number format (`1-to-7`↔`1-7`) but keeps the **leaf exact** — it recovers the proportion near-miss (`IR.sean-anchor.proportion.head-to-body-1-7`) without flattering a wrong leaf. **Clean-FP fix (Sean's call):** a clean fixture (expected pass) that Em wrongly flags scores citation **none**, not credit — retiring the `clean-c06` quirk where any non-empty cite on a false positive scored True. `_block` now reports the split-axis breakdown (graded `cites_correct` mean + full/partial/none counts); `score.py`'s matrix block and per-case detail render the citation axis apart from the verdict axis. **Eval alignment:** the view cases (vd1–4/vb1) now cite `IR.sean.view.declared-view-matches-drawn`; the anatomy cases (ad1–4) cite their 1:1 authored handle — aligning the eval to rules that now exist (verdict labels untouched; ships-red).

**Step 4 — style/geometry handles surfaced in Em's criteria block ([`pipeline/agents/vision_critic.py`](pipeline/agents/vision_critic.py) `_criteria_block`).** The block now leads with the bare handle and explicitly instructs Em to copy the exact `IR.*` ID and **not** substitute a generic HF/SF reason-code or invent a handle — the fix for the construction/shading reason-code substitution (mini-run Q1). Empty-cites invariant left intact (geometry now has citeable handles to survive it).

**Coverage gap logged (not silently dropped).** The 4 per-view rules beyond declared-view (three-quarter / profile / front / back) are **vocabulary-grounding with no eval fixture yet** — authored so Em stops confabulating those handles, but unmeasured. Follow-up: add view fixtures in the next corpus expansion. The 4 anatomy rules and the declared-view rule all have eval coverage.

**Guards green (credential-free).** `tests/` **306 passed**; `evals/vision_critic/runner.py` **58 passed / 6 xpassed**; `pipeline/tests/` **10 passed**; `evals/character_designer/runner.py` **6 passed / 1 xpassed**; `evals/planner/runner.py` **5 passed / 1 xfailed**. ## 2026-06-07 — RAN: Reve-vs-NB2 editing bake-off, live (costed ~$0.77) → Reve FAILS for editing Sean (face morph)

**What & why.** Executed the live Reve-vs-NB2 generator bake-off under fleet-ops discipline (isolated worktree `bakeoff/reve-vs-nb2-editing`, `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` unset → Em on subscription, smoke-before-spend ladder). Decision artifact: [`evals/bakeoffs/2026-06-07-reve-vs-nb2-editing/results.md`](evals/bakeoffs/2026-06-07-reve-vs-nb2-editing/results.md); [field report](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-07-reve-vs-nb2-editing-field-report.md) + [postmortem](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-07-reve-vs-nb2-bakeoff-postmortem.md).

**Verdict (Sean's eyeball, ratified): REVE FAILS for editing the Sean character — NOT adopted at any tier; NB2 stays the editing engine.** The metric and the eye disagreed and the eye won (Engine Truth). DINOv2-vs-per-view-anchor scored Reve ≥ NB2 on identity (decisive `t2-remix-3quarter` +0.041; in-between +0.006; SCR 0/5), which *by the harness rule* would have meant pilot-keyframes + adopt-in-betweens — **but face-crop inspection shows the Reve outputs morph and skew the face** (asymmetric/melted eyes, distorted features) while body/pose/palette/register hold. For an identity-locked character that is disqualifying. **Key methodological finding: DINOv2-vs-full-figure-anchor cannot see facial morph** (face = small fraction of the embedding; Reve matched composition → high cosine on a broken face) — the §3.5 "over-rewards composition, not a sole gate" caveat, confirmed live. Identity edits must be gated on the face by eye / pairwise-Em, not whole-figure DINOv2. The "no NB-Pro *downsampling* regression" composition finding still holds (no washout/collapse), but Reve substitutes its own identity failure. **Future direction (not now): test Reve for new-character creation + backgrounds in other art styles** (no identity to preserve). reve-fast NOT added to the in-between lineup.

**Schema was WRONG as scaffolded — corrected against the live API.** The mirror-inferred Reve schema 400'd on the first live call. Reverse-engineered from the API's structured errors + confirmed calls: Edit `{edit_instruction, reference_image}`, Remix `{prompt, reference_images}`, tier via the `version` param (standard `reve-edit@20250915`/`reve-remix@20250915`, 30cr; fast `reve-edit-fast@20251030`/`reve-remix-fast@20251030`, 5cr — fast strings from Sean's Reve Edit API console doc + empirical remix-fast confirmation), response = flat top-level base64 `image` + `credits_used`/`version`/`content_violation`. `reve_runner.py` patched + committed; refuses fast with an unknown version rather than silently running standard. Added an opt-in, non-scoring `REVE_DEBUG_LOG` metadata hook.

**Operational (report §5 Test 4).** No visible watermark + **no C2PA/JUMBF/XMP markers** in Reve PNGs (clean but unsigned). Pencil-test register **not** content-filtered (0 violations / 9 live calls). Latency: standard 20–26s, fast 11–14s (~2×). No rate-limit headers surfaced; 0× 429. **Spend ≈ $0.77** (275 Reve credits ~$0.37 + ~6 NB2 imgs ~$0.40; ~35% over the $0.57 plan, all schema-discovery tax). Snapshots pinned in `variants.yaml`. **t3 validity edit:** stand-in turnaround crops → genuine approved Act-1 keyframes PT_A1_F06→F10 (committed fixtures; `runs/` is gitignored), applied pre-scoring (ships-red). **Harness gap filed:** `bakeoff.py` silently records a non-ok `ReveResponse` (HTTP 400) as a clean non-stub cell — should fail loud (not fixed this run to avoid mid-spend harness churn). Guardrails honored: subscription billing, worktree isolation, singleton pre-flight, DINOv2 tier verified (`dinov2`, not `pil-perceptual`), clean teardown.

## 2026-06-07 — Scaffold: Reve-vs-NB2 editing bake-off (built, smoke-validated in stub, NOT yet run)

**What & why.** Built the dated bake-off that turns the evaluation report's §5 test protocol into runnable code: [`evals/bakeoffs/2026-06-07-reve-vs-nb2-editing/`](evals/bakeoffs/2026-06-07-reve-vs-nb2-editing/). It answers the one question desk research left open — *does Reve hold Sean's identity under a real multi-reference edit at least as well as NB2, and does it suffer the multi-reference downsampling failure that demoted NB Pro?* Scaffolded against the existing T2 bake-off conventions and the method locked by [`docs/research/2026-05-31-ai-evals-best-practices-and-anima-eval-strategy.md`](docs/research/2026-05-31-ai-evals-best-practices-and-anima-eval-strategy.md).

**Shape — a GENERATOR bake-off, not a judge bake-off.** The 2026-05-31 shoot-out varied the model that runs *Em*; this varies the model that *produces the edit* and scores the outputs. Three variants (`nb2` incumbent / `reve-standard` / `reve-fast`) edit five cases (Tests 1–3: single-ref expression edit, the multi-ref **downsampling probe** `t2-remix-3quarter`, the 3-ref A-7 attribute-bleed probe, and an in-between). Two stages: `generate` → `score`.

**Metric contract (eval-strategy §3.5 + §6 generator row), encoded not narrated:** DINOv2-vs-**per-view-anchor** is the headline (reuses the shipped `similarity_gate.compute_similarity` ladder; each case names its same-view anchor — never score a 3/4 output against the front anchor); **no universal DINO threshold → the decision is the Reve-vs-NB2 Δ** on the same case+anchor; Subject-Collapse below-threshold **count** (not a mean) + `stderr()` per variant; in-betweens score against both endpoints and take the **min** (collapse floor). **Em is secondary** (`--score-em`, reference-blind absolute) — a still-image judge is trustworthy mainly pairwise, so DINOv2 decides and pairwise-Em is flagged as the documented refinement, not faked.

**Fleet-ops + cost-safety baked in.** `--stub` HARD short-circuits the runners (it never calls a model — important because `invoke_image_edit` reads `.env` directly, so a populated `.env` would otherwise fire a real costed NB2 call under `--stub`; this was a bug caught and fixed during the smoke test). `--score-em` refuses to run if `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is set (subscription-billing guard, mirroring `score.py`). README documents the isolated-worktree / keys / DINOv2-install runbook.

**Honesty flags carried in-repo:** (1) `reve_runner.py`'s endpoint schema is **inferred from third-party mirrors**, not first-party-verified (Reve's console docs are an auth-gated SPA) — the operator must verify every `_REVE_*` constant + pin the returned model header before the live run; (2) Test 3 uses turnaround-crop stand-in endpoints — swap in two genuine approved adjacent anchors for the real run; (3) `results.md` ships as an explicit **"not yet run" placeholder** (raw traces + manifest gitignored) — a scaffold that says so beats a stub matrix that looks real. Smoke-validated `--stage all --stub` green (exit 0, all 3 variants produce outputs, scoring runs); **pytest contract-suite + fixture-contamination run owed on Sean's machine** (no venv/pytest in the build sandbox; the scaffold is isolated to the new bakeoff dir and touches nothing under `tests/`/`pipeline/`/`fixtures/`).

## 2026-06-07 — Research doc: Reve & Ideogram 4 evaluation for the editing layer (desk research, no model spend)

**What & why.** Two newly-released image models (Reve, closed API; Ideogram 4, claimed open-source) came up as possible adoptions into anima's editing layer (Phase 5 Generate, Phase 6 cleanup, Cy's Phase 2 Bible plates), benchmarked against the incumbent NB2 (`gemini-3.1-flash-image-preview`). Ran a cited desk-research evaluation — no paid API calls, no local inference — written to [`docs/research/2026-06-07-reve-ideogram4-evaluation.md`](docs/research/2026-06-07-reve-ideogram4-evaluation.md).

**Findings (load-bearing).**
- **Ideogram 4 — PASS on all three use cases.** Authenticity *verified*: `ideogram-oss/ideogram4` is a genuine Ideogram, Inc. release (interlocks with the official `ideogram-ai` HF org, the company blog, a coherent legal license naming Ideogram Inc., and the real hiring board) — not a name-squat, not malware. But two facts disqualify it: (1) the weights ship under a **Non-Commercial Model Agreement** ([license](https://github.com/ideogram-oss/ideogram4/blob/main/model_licenses/LICENSE-IDEOGRAM-4-NON-COMMERCIAL)) that excludes promoting revenue-generating work — anima's portfolio purpose sits outside the grant; (2) it is **text-to-image only** — no editing, inpaint, img2img, or reference/identity conditioning, so it structurally cannot do Cy's job. Local feasibility also fails independently: the 9.3B DiT + 8B Qwen3-VL text encoder is a **24GB-class** model (marginal-to-infeasible on the RTX 5080's 16GB), atop unresolved Blackwell `sm_120` PyTorch-wheel friction. **Do not run locally; do not adopt.**
- **Reve — SUPPLEMENT (pilot, don't yet adopt).** Right shape: genuine instruction-Edit + 1–6-reference Remix, 16:9 native, ~2K resolution, **full commercial rights + user-owned outputs** (the opposite of Ideogram's wall). Cost is the headline win — Reve Fast ~$0.007/edit vs NB2 ~$0.067/image at 1024px (**~10× cheaper**; independently corroborated ~$667 vs ~$6,700 per 100k). The catch: the exact failure that demoted NB Pro — **multi-reference downsampling / identity loss** — is *unmeasured* on Reve; its consistency claims are vendor marketing. Gate adoption on a head-to-head SF02/SF01 identity test vs NB2 before trusting it with keyframes; in-betweens are the strongest first fit.
- **Cost answer.** Reve is cheaper per image than NB2 at *every* tier → no break-even threshold; absolute saving is modest at hobby volume (single-digit to low-tens $/mo), material only if still-frame in-between volume scales.

**Deliverable.** Full report with TL;DR, decision table, sections A–D, an authenticity/safety callout box, a hands-on test protocol (Sean-anchor + A-7 multi-ref edit scored through Em, logged as a dated `evals/bakeoffs/` run), and an open-questions list. **Source caveat flagged in-doc:** Reve's first-party console docs are an auth-gated JS SPA — first-party detail leans on Sean's pricing screenshots + third-party API mirrors. No code, manifest, criteria, or baseline touched.

## 2026-06-06 — G6 step 2: Em references re-test ADOPTED (prior 2026-06-04 run re-landed clean) — safety holds, precision cost is rule-scoping, flag stays off

**What & why.** G6 sequence step 2 (instrumented mini-run ✅ → **references re-test** → G6.1 citation grounding) per [`docs/2026-06-04-em-references-retest-handoff.md`](docs/2026-06-04-em-references-retest-handoff.md). The re-test was **already executed N=5 on 2026-06-04** (branch `feature/em-references-retest`, commit `9df54b9`) but pushed-and-never-merged, on the 50-case corpus (the handoff's literal ask) before the corpus-complete merge (#26) grew it to 52. Sean's call this session: **adopt that run as decisive — do NOT re-spend on a fresh live run** (the references-vs-blind gate sits on the same 44 G5 `performs` cases either way; the two later additions, `proportion-pb1`/`palette-pad4`, are informational defect cases that cannot move the decision). This entry re-lands the prior run's evidence **clean onto current 52-main**: it keeps the handoff brief the prior branch wrongly deleted, drops the premature CLAUDE.md edit the prior branch carried (the Em-row update is Sean-ratified separately), and supersedes the stale branch. **No model spend this session.**

**The result (references-ON, N=5 majority, vs the ratified reference-blind G5 baseline; `performs` n=44).**
- **Safety HELD — the load-bearing result.** `false_pass 0.00` (= blind) and `recall 1.00` (= blind); all 28 single-axis defects caught (FN=0). The 2026-06-02 false-pass regression (0.00→0.15) **did not reproduce** → **confirmed fixture-borne** (the old "clean" cases were SHA-identical reference plates; [`tests/test_fixture_contamination.py`](tests/test_fixture_contamination.py) now forbids that by construction).
- **Precision 0.97 → 0.85 as rule-enforcement, not confabulation.** 5 clean FPs vs blind's 1; 4 of 5 (c02/c03/c05/c13) fail because the attached criteria block surfaces `IR.sean.prop.stylus-right-hand-always` (a production stylus-continuity rule, cited in 37/50 cases — a "cite magnet") onto clean fixtures that depict no stylus, with `cites_correct=yes`. c06 = HF03 orientation + stylus (also the lone blind FP; references did **not** fix it).
- **Citation grounding fixed:** `cites-correct 0.03 → 0.73`; geometry empty-cites invariant trips 3/250 → 0/250. The residual misses are view/anatomy, whose expected handles aren't authored IR rules yet — exactly the G6.1 gap.
- **Decision against the brief's §rules: flag stays OFF** — fails the `precision ≥ 0.97` flip-gate. But this is **not** a "confirmed-real regression, stop relitigating references": references make grounding work, and the only regression (precision) is an eval-corpus / rule-scoping interaction (a continuity-prop rule imported into a single-frame consistency eval), not confabulation. Re-openable after G6.1 authors real view/anatomy IR rules **and** the stylus-rule scoping is resolved. **Sean ratifies before any CLAUDE.md / flag change.** `clean-c06` stays red (ships-red; G6.1 view-rule acceptance case).

**Tooling added ($0, no live calls): `--attach-references` CLI override** (`evals/vision_critic/score.py`). The prior run enabled references via a temporary worktree manifest edit (reverted before commit); the handoff requires a run-scoped flag instead so references can **never** be enabled by committing `attach_references: true`. The flag mutates the in-memory manifest only (repo default stays `false`) and is **propagated into each per-case worker**, so the orchestrator's `refs=` trace label can never claim references a blind worker didn't actually attach. New mocked tests [`tests/test_score_attach_references.py`](tests/test_score_attach_references.py) (engages-bundle / default-blind / subprocess-propagation anti-lie). Guards green: `tests/` **305 passed**, `evals/vision_critic/runner.py` **53 passed / 6 xpassed**.

**50→52 reconciliation.** The adopted field report + trace are a faithful 50-case record, kept **byte-identical** (field report `1c68b6a…`, trace `bad48fd…`). The corpus is now 52; the references-vs-blind gate is computed on the 44 `performs` cases G5 measured, unchanged by the two later additions. A future replicated run (the G6.1 re-baseline) folds `pb1`/`pad4` in.

**CLAUDE.md Em-row RATIFIED (Sean, 2026-06-06).** The row's references-grounding section was rewritten to retire the now-void **confabulation** diagnosis (and its contaminated `0.62→0.73` figures) and record the clean-corpus re-test: regression confirmed **fixture-borne**, safety held (false_pass 0.00 / recall 1.00), citations fixed (0.03→0.73), the lone cost precision 0.97→0.85 diagnosed as **stylus-rule scoping**. The re-open condition is now explicit and **two-part**: (a) scope `IR.sean.prop.stylus-right-hand-always` so it doesn't fire where no stylus is depictable, AND (b) G6.1 authors real `view.*`/`anatomy.*-count` IR rules. DINOv2 reframed superseded-pending (its references half is answered; final call after SF03).

**Instrumentation (code).**
- `evals/vision_critic/scoring.py`: `CaseScore` gains a `reasoning: str = ""` field (last, defaulted — positional ctors + the `asdict`↔`CaseScore(**…)` subprocess round-trip stay back-compatible; never scored).
- `evals/vision_critic/score.py`: `_score_one` captures `reasoning`; `consensus_scores` preserves it from the majority-matching run; new pure `render_per_case_detail()` renders a per-case cites/`cites_correct`/reasoning section (always-on — additive, no metric effect); new `--trace-name LABEL` writes ONLY `traces/{LABEL}.md` and leaves `last-run.md` + the dated baseline trace untouched (so a same-day diagnostic can't clobber the ratified baseline).
- `pipeline/agents/vision_critic.py`: the empty-cites invariant now raises a typed **`EmptyCitesInvariant(ValueError)`** carrying the parsed payload (verdict/reasoning/cites). **Production behavior unchanged** — it still raises (the critic spine still rejects an ungrounded block), and subclassing `ValueError` keeps every `except ValueError` / `pytest.raises(ValueError, match="cites_criteria")` site valid. The score.py `--only` worker catches this exact subclass (DIAGNOSTIC only) and records the reasoning flagged `[INVARIANT_TRIPPED]`, so a geometry trip becomes captured data instead of a blind errored gap (Option B). New test `tests/test_em_score_report.py::test_render_per_case_detail_surfaces_cites_and_reasoning`. `tests/` 302 passed + eval runner 51 passed/6 xpassed; `--stub` proven $0 (all-STUB verdicts).

**Findings (the verdict layer reproduced G5; the diagnostic was the cites layer).**
- **Performs n=44: precision 0.97 / recall 1.00 / false_pass 0.00, cites-correct 0.03** — a single N=1 pass landed the G5 N=5 numbers; all 28 single-axis defects caught, lone FP `clean-c06`. (Motion 5/6 flagged, `motion-t2-arc` the lone slip — carried from G5.)

(1) **proportion** = matcher-recoverable: Em names the right leaf (`head-to-body`) but confabulates the namespace/format (`IR.sean-anchor.…-1-7` vs the real, existing `IR.sean.proportion.head-to-body-1-to-7`). (2) **construction/shading** = real vocabulary gap: Em substitutes the manifest QA codes (`HF05`/`SF01`) and never cites the existing `IR.sean.style.*` handle. (3) **view/anatomy** = no IR rule exists in the Bible to cite (22 rules, zero view/zero anatomy); Em invents structured `IR.sean-anchor.view.*` / `…anatomy.*-count` handles — which are the exact templates for G6.1 authoring.
- **clean-c06** flagged borderline@0.95 on an orientation/facing read ("facing screen-right instead of screen-left") — a view-correctness/facing-convention seam, not register or identity. **Recommend: keep as known disagreement, no relabel** (ships-red discipline); it's the canonical test case for the G6.1 view IR rule.
- All three cites failure modes are addressed by **G6.1 (geometry IR criteria + split verdict/citation scoring)**; this run hands G6.1 Em's exact handle vocabulary to author against, and argues the split-scorer should credit a correct manifest reason-code as partial grounding.

**What & why.** Executed the staged G5 handoff — the first Em baseline on a contamination-guarded foundation. `python -m evals.vision_critic.score --runs 5`, N=5 majority vote, reference-blind (`attach_references: false`), `gemini-3.5-flash` pinned by ID via the `gemini_api` transport + Opus 4.7 escalation, in an isolated worktree with `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` absent and the bounded `GEMINI_API_KEY` from `.env`. **247/250 case-runs scored** (3 sporadic empty-cites errors, all recovered by majority — zero total gaps); no quota-throttling. Em caught **all 28 single-axis defects across all six classes** (recall 1.00, FN=0) and never false-passed a defect; the lone error is one clean false-positive (`clean-c06`, flagged fail all 5 runs → precision 0.97). Reference-blind Em is a strong verdict engine — vindicates keeping references off by default. **Sean-ratified 2026-06-04; the CLAUDE.md Critic Stack + Em row now carry the figures + caveats, retiring the void baseline.**
- **The asterisk — cites-correct = 0.03.** Verdicts are right; citations almost never match the expected criterion. Partly by eval construction (geometry classes carry declared-seam handles that aren't IR rules in Em's merged criteria — she cannot cite what she wasn't given), partly possibly real on style classes (needs per-case cite inspection in G6). The headline metric contract is unaffected, but for a critic that "proposes fixes grounded in criteria," the grounding is the weak axis. **Top G6 input.**
- **Geometry classes trip the empty-cites invariant** (`proportion-pd3`, `view-vb1`, `anatomy-ad1` — 3/250 case-runs). Em detects the geometry defect (caught 13/13) but returns a blocking verdict with empty `cites_criteria`; the v2 §2.3 Pattern B safety invariant rejects it. Same disease as cites-correct=0.03: a *production* safety rule (no uncited blocks) eats *eval* signal (Em did see it). Sporadic → majority recovered every verdict. G6 to decide: give geometry citeable IR criteria, or record verdict separately from citation.
- **Motion: Em flagged 5/6 — a finding, not a win.** Against the "expected 0 catches" ships-red framing, Em caught five via **spatial traces** in the contact-sheet frames (jitter/flicker/texture-crawl), not motion perception. The lone slip — `motion-t2-arc` (pure timing, no per-frame tell) — is the true contact-sheet blind spot. Reframes (doesn't invalidate) the ships-red expectation. false_pass band (motion) 0.17–0.33.
- **Variance majority-resolved.** 7/50 cases flipped across runs (model variance the brief predicted); the N=5 false_pass band makes it visible: performs 0.00–0.04, overall 0.03–0.09 — the performs safety number is stable in every single run.
- **Provenance.** Foundation (G1–G4) + the pre-flight mock-fix committed first on branch `eval/em-rebaseline-g5` (commits `b7323e3`, `71f8d80`); the baseline ran against that committed, reproducible state, not mutable working-tree. Two corpus slots (P-B1, PA-D4) remain pending Sean re-rolls — excluded by design; they add two cases, not a re-baseline.

## 2026-06-04 — Fix: runner.py mock cost-leak (gemini_api transport), caught in G5 pre-flight

**What & why.** `evals/vision_critic/runner.py`'s `_patch_em_runners` stubbed only `run_antigravity_with_image` (the legacy `agy` transport) and Opus — never `run_gemini_api_with_image`. So the "credential-free mocked plumbing" suite fired **real, costed Gemini calls** on any machine with a key present — staying "green in CI" only because CI has no key (the runner self-stubs when the key is absent). Surfaced during the G5 re-baseline pre-flight: the suite hung ~13 min on an ESTABLISHED TCP to a Google IP with near-zero CPU. **Fix:** also patch `pipeline.agents.vision_critic.run_gemini_api_with_image`. ## 2026-06-03 — Eval-foundation reset: fixture corpus spec + gold-standard turnarounds (Sean character)

**What & why.** The foundation-first plan (entry below) reaches the authoring stage. Sean re-authored the `sean-anchor` gold-standard turnarounds in the 2D Disney pencil-test register via Nano Banana 2 in Google Flow, and the class-isolated fixture corpus is now specced. No pipeline code; prompt + spec artifacts only.

- **Gold-standard turnarounds (re-authored, trusted).** `prompts/eval-corpus/sean-anchor-turnaround-sheet.md` — the proven SFII/pixel turnaround prompt restyled to pencil-test-colored, identity markers enumerated, and the **1:7 proportion lock** added (this is the A4 gold-standard *source*; the reset exists because proportion drifted to ~1:4–1:5.3). Split into **two sheets** (full-body carries proportion + views; head carries face/construction/expression) after the combined layout overcrowded and fought the height lock. Both rendered at 1:7 across all five views and ratified by Sean. **Resolution decision: 1K, not 2K** — the 2K download is an exact 2× upscale (mean-abs-diff 4.18/255 vs the native 1K downscaled; ~13% *less* high-frequency grit), and the upscale smooths exactly the construction-line / cross-hatch cues two of our six classes depend on. MLLM judges downsample anyway. Uniform 1K corpus-wide to avoid a resolution confound.

- **Three structural decisions locked (Sean, 2026-06-03):** (1) **one shared clean pool** as the universal negative for all six classes (a clean plate is clean for every class at once); (2) **paired** clean/defect by default (same pose, one axis flipped → unambiguous attribution); (3) **generate-first** via NB2, hand-drawing reserved for the borderline near-misses (and any defect NB2's identity-preservation won't hold). NB2-generated fixtures are a feature, not a confound — production frames are themselves NB2-generated, so the corpus matches the distribution Em judges.

- **Fixture corpus spec.** `prompts/eval-corpus/sean-anchor-fixture-corpus.md` — 45 Sean fixtures (16 shared clean + 24 defect + 5 hand-drawn borderlines), ~5/class across the six ratified classes. **Open flag for Sean:** *anatomy-count* is natively a mascot class (nub count); for the human it's interpreted as hand/digit/limb correctness — pending his confirm/redirect/drop. Mascot corpus deferred until it has its own turnaround.

- **Corpus prompts rewritten to v2 (minimal grammar) after a 4-prompt Flow test falsified the v1 scaffold.** The v1 five-slot scaffold (verbose identity enumeration + keep-lists + sheet vocabulary) violated the NB2 editing doc's own headline finding — terse text + strong reference beats verbose prose. Empirically: the v1 clean prompt's sheet-language pushed NB2 into model-sheet mode (3 panels + ladder lines instead of a keyframe); the v1 palette defect held the shirt but degraded the desk; Sean's minimal prompt produced the best output of the four with zero identity words. v2 grammar: *opener + one beat/pose + view/framing + (defects: one corruption clause) + the fixed style-maintain line* — references carry identity, text carries only the delta. Two structural rules: when a defect targets a phrase the style line asserts (cross-hatch, color wash), that phrase is removed from the style line in that prompt; and **view-correctness defects need no corruption clause at all** — the image is a clean drawing of the wrong view, the defect lives in the case's declared view in `cases.yaml`. All 45 prompts now ship fully assembled, copy-paste-ready for Flow.

## 2026-06-03 — Eval-foundation reset: verified the diagnosis, planned the clean foundation (orient-and-decide, no spend)

**What & why.** A week of individually-sound eval work kept returning NO-GOs (reference-grounding regression, DINOv2, proportion-measure). Root cause confirmed this session: the eval foundation — the fixtures and the Bible they reference — is unsound, so every measurement was noisy or vacuous. This is a deliberate step back to fix the ruler before measuring again. Decision artifact: [`docs/2026-06-03-eval-foundation-reset-plan.md`](docs/2026-06-03-eval-foundation-reset-plan.md). No code, no model spend.

- **Diagnosis verified against the tree (all four defects confirmed; two worse than hypothesized).** (1) **Contaminated fixtures** — 19 of 23 `evals/vision_critic/fixtures/frames/*.png` are SHA-256-identical copies of Bible/source plates, spanning *all three* label classes (clean/borderline/defect), not just defects; only `clean_F06/F13/F31` + `defect_F13_stylus_hand`/`defect_F31_scale` are independent. Mechanism correction: byte-identical copies (distinct inode), not hardlinks to the Bible. This is the by-construction cause of the 2026-06-02 reference-grounding confabulation regression — "clean" cases literally ARE reference plates. (2) **Drifted ground truth** — `sean-anchor` body turnarounds locked at ~1:4–1:5.3 heads-tall vs 1:7 (corroborated by SF03 doc + pixel-grounded Cy verdicts). (3) **Stacked defects** — 5 fail-cases carry compound labels. (4) **Tiny, unbalanced n** — 29 cases (15/10/4), ~18 mostly-singleton defect labels; the 2026-06-01 ratification happened against the contaminated set and is retired. The contaminated baseline (precision 0.62 / recall 1.00 / false_pass 0.15) is declared untrustworthy.

- **Error-analysis-first taxonomy, open-coded from 74 real `plate_verdicts.jsonl` records** (not guessed top-down). Sean ratified a **six-class** single-axis corpus scope (2026-06-03): proportion, palette, view-correctness, anatomy-count, construction-lines, shading-register. Per-identity-feature modes (hair-silhouette, jaw-geometry, eye/brow) **deliberately deferred** this round, reversible with a promotion trigger.

- **Layer-ownership map locked (Sean, 2026-06-03): geometry → Bible-lock (deterministic), style/identity → Em (MLLM).** proportion + view-correctness + anatomy-count are owned by the deterministic Bible-lock gate at author-time; palette + construction-lines + shading-register are owned by Em/T2 per production frame. Stops asking Em to catch proportion (DINOv2 NO-GO: embeddings see identity, not geometry) and stops asking the lock to judge shading. **CLAUDE.md update pending Sean's approval of the plan doc** (the layer map is a source-of-truth change).

- **Foundation-first sequence with gates:** clean Bible (A4 re-bake → 1:7, re-locked through SF03) → class-isolated independent fixtures (~40–60 imgs, ~5–10/class) → Sean-ratified labels → CI contamination guard (fails on any fixture↔Bible SHA/inode match) → re-establish Em baseline on the trustworthy set (replaces the 0.62/1.00/0.15 figures) → only then resume costed gate work (SF03 build, references, DINOv2). No costed work resumes until the foundation is trustworthy. Hand to Claude Code after Sean review.

## 2026-06-03 — Workstream B1b DINOv2 spike: NO-GO → pivot to a generation-time SF03 proportion gate (design)

**What & why.** Ran the costed-as-compute (\$0 API) DINOv2 separation spike (`evals/vision_critic/dinov2_separation.py`, PR #20) and it returned **NO-GO** for DINOv2 as a view-matched identity/proportion backstop, for two independent reasons: (1) **the references are contaminated** — every performs fixture with an inferable view is byte-identical to its Bible turnaround plate, including the proportion *defects* (`sean-anchor/turnarounds/body-profile-right.png` IS the plate the eval labels `proportion-eyes-body-profile-right`, a Cy fail @1.0). The record-only Pass-2.5 gate let the proportion-drifted body plates bake into the locked Bible, so there is no clean 1:7 per-view reference to compare against. (2) **Embedding similarity is the wrong signal** — proportion defects score 0.82–0.89 vs the anchor (still recognizably Sean); DINOv2 cosine captures identity/style, not head-to-body geometry.

A follow-on dependency-free silhouette landmark spike (PIL+numpy, inline) also returned **NO-GO**: chin detection across multi-view stylized line art is fragile (detection noise ≈ the 4.6-vs-5.5-head signal; back/¾ views confound the neck-narrowing).

**Decisions (Sean, 2026-06-03):**
- DINOv2-as-proportion-backstop is dead; `attach_references` stays **off** (no deterministic partner emerged). B1c/B2/B3 superseded.
- **Pivot to a generation-time, reference-free SF03 proportion gate** — constrain proportion against a known armature at generation, verify the render against it (the animatic analog), instead of reverse-engineering it from finished art. **Design-only this round** (changes Cy's generation contract); **scoped to Cy Pass-3 / Bible-lock**, where proportion drift originates and volume is tiny — NOT per-frame T2/Em. Design: [`docs/2026-06-03-sf03-proportion-gate-design.md`](docs/2026-06-03-sf03-proportion-gate-design.md).
- **Bible-integrity escalation** filed on the A4 ticket: `sean-anchor`'s body turnarounds are proportion-off (not just Flash-verified) and need a 1:7 re-bake; the Em eval fixtures derived from them are SHA-contaminated and must be re-derived + labels re-ratified once the Bible is clean.

**Also landed this session:** B1a view-aware reference selection (PR #19, below) and the recovery of Workstream A onto `main` (PR #18 had merged but a stale local checkout hid it — synced, no re-land needed).

## 2026-06-02 — Workstream B1a: view-aware reference selection (approach A, eval path)

**What & why.** The DINOv2 identity/proportion backstop (Workstream B) needs **per-view references** to be meaningful — a single front anchor can't separate legitimate view variation from drift, which is exactly why the Pass-2.5 similarity gate is record-only. This lands the prerequisite: `pipeline/agents/reference_selection.py` now reads the subject's view from the beat and ranks the matching turnaround first, so a profile subject gets a profile reference. Uncosted, deterministic, dormant behind `critics.t2.attach_references` (still default-off) — it changes *which* references attach when references are on, nothing else.

- **`_infer_view(beat)`** — phrase-based view inference (`"right profile"` → `profile-right`, `"3/4 turnaround"` → `3quarter`, `"back view"` → `back`, …). Phrase-keyed on purpose: a bare `"side"`/`"back"`/`"front"` would false-match common words (`"background"`, `"beside"`). Returns the view **token** (a substring of the turnaround stems), or `None`.
- **`_view_aware_preference(view)`** — reorders the existing diversity preference so view-matching patterns lead; `None` reproduces the approach-B order **exactly** (the viewless path is unchanged — the locked `test_real_sean_bible_target_bundle` still holds).
- **`select_references(...)`** — now threads `beat` through `_infer_view` → `_view_aware_preference` → `_select_turnarounds(folder, cap, preference)`. `checkpoint` stays a reserved seam.
- **`best_view_reference(character_id, beat, *, characters_root)`** (new) — the single best view-matched turnaround the DINOv2 backstop (B1b/B1c) will compare the subject against. `None` when no view is inferable or no plate matches that view (then there is no view-fair reference; the caller skips the deterministic check rather than compare across views). Sorted order puts `body-*` before `head-*`, so a full-figure proportion subject gets a body reference — what proportion similarity needs.

**Scope (honest).** Delivers the **eval path** — the subject's view is read from case metadata (cheap + exact; the cases carry it: `beat "Sean full-body right profile"`). **Production view-inference** (no guaranteed labeled view — a cheap view classifier or a manifest hint) is a separate, harder follow-on, deliberately out of scope.

**Verification.** `tests/test_reference_selection.py` +6, `tests/test_vision_critic_references.py` +1 (view-matched plate leads the turnarounds through Em). Contract suite `tests/` **298 green** (was 291), `pipeline/tests/` 10 green, credential-free. No model spend.

## 2026-06-02 — Em provenance + hardening bundle (Workstream A): references flag-gated off, model pinned-by-ID at both costed call sites, stale "Pro" labels corrected, scorer replication

**What & why.** The re-baseline below produced two consequential results: (1) the obviously-good reference-grounding change MEASURED as a regression (false_pass 0.00→0.15), and (2) a validity gate caught that agy ran with no `-m` flag, so the Antigravity backend silently chose the model (gemini-3.5-flash) on 272/272 Em-sized calls while every label claimed "3.1 Pro" — and the same wrapper verified Cy's two locked Bibles. Sean's locked decisions (2026-06-02): gate references off behind a flag; fix provenance code + labels now (uncosted) and defer costed Bible re-verification to a ticket; promote DINOv2 to the next costed workstream; replicate the baseline (N=5, majority vote, false_pass band). This is the uncosted hardening bundle (Workstream A) — one CI-green PR; the costed DINOv2 spike + replicated re-baseline (Workstream B) are a separate greenlit handoff. Full plan: [`docs/2026-06-02-em-provenance-and-hardening-kickoff.md`](docs/2026-06-02-em-provenance-and-hardening-kickoff.md).

- **A1 — references behind a flag, OFF by default.** New `critics.t2.attach_references` (manifest, default `false`). `pipeline/agents/vision_critic.py` reads it via `_attach_references(t2_cfg)`: when false, Em runs reference-blind (no Bible reference bundle, no IR/AC `_criteria_block`) — the safe recall-1.00 / false_pass-0.00 profile. The PR #13 grounding path stays in code, dormant, behind the flag, until DINOv2 + a clean re-baseline clear the false-pass gate. TDD: `tests/test_vision_critic_references_flag.py` (default-blind, explicit-false, true-restores-bundle, shipped-manifest guard); the existing reference/criteria tests now opt in with `attach_references: true`.

- **A2 — pin model by ID + log the model that actually fired (both costed call sites); never silently backend-default again.**
  - **Em (`pipeline/agents/gemini_api_runner.py`):** `_generate` now returns `(text, served_model)` read back from `resp.model_version` (not the pinned constant echoed blindly); `run_gemini_api_with_image` records it on `.model` and logs `served model=… (requested=…)`.
  - **agy wrapper (`pipeline/agents/cli_runners.py`):** `CLIResponse` gains a `model` field; `run_antigravity_with_image` gains `model=` (passed as `-m`, recorded, logged). A real (binary-present) call **without** a model now RAISES — the silent backend-default that mislabeled 272 calls cannot recur unobserved. (agy print-mode stdout can't confirm the served model, so the recorded value is the requested pin — which is *why* Cy moved to the API; see below.)
  - **Cy (`pipeline/agents/character_designer.py`):** Pass-3 verification routed from `run_antigravity_with_image` → `run_gemini_api_with_image` (the confirmable transport: pins gemini-3.5-flash by ID, reads `resp.model_version` back, logs it). Behavior-preserving (Flash is what agy actually served) and fleet-ops-aligned (bounded `GEMINI_API_KEY` vs agy's personal OAuth). Dodges the unverifiable `agy -m` flag (the findings doc contradicts itself on v1.0.2 support).
  - TDD: `tests/test_model_provenance.py` (served-model read-back, both runners log their model, agy-real-call-without-model raises, costed success never returns an empty model). Existing gemini_api + rate-cap + character_designer tests updated for the new contracts.

- **A3 — corrected stale "Pro" labels** on the live behavioral surfaces (the fleet/models read these as truth): `manifest.yaml` `default_model` (→ `gemini-3.5-flash`) + the T2 comment; the Em + Cy rows in CLAUDE.md; the agent-module docstrings (`vision_critic.py`, `cli_runners.py`, `character_designer.py`); Cy's Pass-3 verifier prompt (made model-neutral — a hardcoded model identity is what let the drift hide); the two standing-context prompts (`anima-standing-context.md`, `cy-character-designer-context.md`); the two eval READMEs. **Left intact** as dated evidence: CHANGELOG history, research/postmortem/cowork docs, the already-honest forensic comments. **Flagged to Sean (not edited unilaterally per the locked-labels rule):** the 2026-05-31 bake-off labels (`evals/bakeoffs/.../variants.yaml`, `bakeoff.py` — kickoff defers bake-off relabeling to B3), the test-fixture `default_model` values (cosmetic, no code reads them), and `evals/vision_critic/failure-modes.md`'s example label.

- **A4 — filed the costed Cy Bible re-verification ticket** in `code-brain/vault/00_inbox/tickets.md` (re-verify sean-anchor + claude-mascot Pass-3 on a pinned model; they were Flash-verified, not Pro; scheduled after this PR; decide Flash-as-shipped vs a deliberate 3.1-pro upgrade).

- **A5 — replication in the costed scorer (`evals/vision_critic/score.py`).** New `--runs N` (default 1; the real baseline runs `--runs 5`). The point estimate uses the per-case **majority verdict** across runs; `last-run.md` reports a per-segment false_pass **band** (min/max ± stderr across runs) plus a **per-run verdict table** that flags FLIPs — so the run-to-run variance the single estimate hides (the Opus variance the re-baseline diagnosed) is visible, not silently averaged away. Pure helpers (`majority_verdict`, `consensus_scores`, `false_pass_band`, `render_per_run_table`) are TDD-pinned in `tests/test_score_replication.py`. Also folded in the A1 trace-honesty fix: the scorer's `refs=[…]` log now reads `blind` when `attach_references` is off, so the trace never lists refs Em didn't see.

**Verification.** Contract suite `tests/` **291 green** (was 275; +16 across A1/A2/A5), credential-free; `evals/vision_critic/runner.py` 30 passed / 6 xpassed; `evals/character_designer/runner.py` 6 passed / 1 xpassed; `pipeline/tests/` 10 passed. No model spend — Workstream B (DINOv2 spike + replicated re-baseline + bake-off re-run) is a separate greenlit handoff.

## 2026-06-02 — Em re-baseline MEASURED via Gemini-API transport — references change BLOCKED by the false-pass gate

**What changed (code):** a new Gemini delivery transport for Em, config-selectable, so the twice-deferred live re-baseline could run when agy's personal-tier Gemini quota kept 429-walling repeated calls.
- **`pipeline/agents/gemini_api_runner.py`** (new) — `run_gemini_api_with_image`, a drop-in for the agy wrapper (`run_antigravity_with_image`): same `(*, prompt, image_paths, timeout_s)` signature, same `.text` response, same `RateCapExhausted` honesty contract (empty/quota → raise, never silent borderline), stub-fallback for credential-free CI. Calls Gemini directly via `google-genai` + `GEMINI_API_KEY` (a separate vendor billing line from agy's Google personal OAuth). Pins `GEMINI_VISION_MODEL`.
- **`pipeline/agents/vision_critic.py`** — transport selector `_vision_transport(t2_cfg)` reads `critics.t2.transport: agy | gemini_api` (defaults to `agy` to preserve prior behavior). References, criteria, and the Opus-SDK escalation are untouched — the transport only delivers images+prompt.
- **`manifest.yaml`** — `critics.t2.transport: gemini_api` set as the project default (agy keeps 429-blocking). **The transport pivot is kept** — it's orthogonal to the references finding and is what made the measurement possible.
- **`evals/vision_critic/score.py`** — `--stub` now forces the credential-free path for both transports; `model_label` reflects the active transport + the real model. +11 contract tests (`tests/test_gemini_api_runner.py`, `test_vision_critic_transport.py`, `test_score_stub_transports.py`); suite **275 green**.

**Forensics correction (the validity gate, verified):** agy passes **no `-m` flag**, so its print-mode Em calls logged `model=""` and the Antigravity backend default ran. Across **272/272 Em-sized agy calls** — spanning the 2026-06-01 0.62 baseline *and* the 2026-06-02 attempts — the propagated model was **"Gemini 3.5 Flash (Medium)"**, never Pro (no `settings.json` pin). So the manifest/docs/CLAUDE.md `gemini-3.1-pro-via-anti-gravity` label was **aspirational** — the 0.62 baseline ran on **gemini-3.5-flash**. To hold the model constant (one variable: transport agy→API), the transport pins `gemini-3.5-flash` (Sean confirmed). Knock-on: the 2026-05-31 bake-off's "Gemini" column was Flash too. The cosmetic `critics.t2.default_model` label is annotated, not changed (no code reads it).

**The measured result (performs, n=23; gemini-3.5-flash@gemini_api + Opus escalation):** false_pass_rate **0.00 → 0.15**, recall **1.00 → 0.85**, precision 0.62 → 0.73 (lift **disqualified** — bought with false passes). **Per §9 this is a worse Em → the references change is BLOCKED, and follow-on #3 (DINOv2 deterministic identity backstop) is promoted from deferred to next.**

**Why (false passes investigated + prompt-ablation):** (1) **verdict variance** — `stylus-hand-f13-cc01` (Opus-escalated, stochastic) scored `pass` in the run but `fail` (correct) on a plain re-run, so a single 24-case run is a noisy false_pass estimate; (2) **confabulation/forgiveness** — `proportion-eyes-body-profile-right` passed consistently, with Opus reciting the reference bundle's pencil register (*"cream paper substrate with visible grain"*) onto a flat-digital fixture that has none. A prompt-ablation (stripping *"a feature that MATCHES the references is correct…"*) flipped it to fail but **for the wrong rule** while still confabulating the register — so the matching-wording is a forgiveness lever, **not a fix**. Recorded levers for future: soften the matching-wording; view-aware reference selection (approach A) for profile shots.

**Open decision (flagged, not acted on):** references-attach is the *shipped* default (PR #13) and is now eval-blocked — revert / gate / await-DINOv2 is Sean's scoping call. **Bake-off NOT run** (gated on a clean re-baseline). Full arc + matrix: [field report postscript](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-02-em-reference-images-field-report.md); artifacts `evals/vision_critic/last-run.md` + `traces/baseline-2026-06-02-scored.md`. Branch `eval/em-rebaseline`: `59b095c` `27f3358` `0cb37eb` `d7d136a`.

## 2026-06-02 — Incident #2 CLEARED: agy is MCP-free

`agy` no longer auto-loads MCP servers on anima's vision-critic path. **Diagnosis corrections (verified on `agy` v1.0.2):** there is no per-invocation config/MCP flag and no `agy inspect`/`/mcp` subcommand (management is via `agy plugin list/enable/disable`), so the originally-scoped surgical "isolated config-dir" (Option A) was unreachable; and the servers were configured in `~/.gemini/settings.json`'s `mcpServers` block (not a separate `mcp_config.json`), with `agy plugin list` empty. **Fix:** since Sean doesn't use MCP in Antigravity, the `mcpServers` block was emptied to `{}` (removed `notebooklm-mcp` + `pencil`; all other settings untouched; backup `~/.gemini/settings.json.bak.1780411432`). **Verified:** `agy -p` spawns zero MCP children across 17 samples; the notebooklm/pencil/obsidian processes a `ps` grep catches are parented by Claude.app / Claude Code in the Antigravity IDE, not `agy`. `pipeline/agents/agy-config/README.md` updated to record the no-flag finding; the stale `agy inspect` reference in `docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md` corrected to `agy plugin list`. **Gate:** conditions #1 (billing) and #2 (MCP-free) for the deferred Em re-baseline are both satisfied; only #3's run-time hygiene (live-process sweep + `stash@{0}` decision) remains.

## 2026-06-02 — Operational incidents: env hardening before any further costed run

**Context:** the Em reference-images workstream shipped its code (264 green, n=1 live-proven) but its repeated *live* attempts surfaced three operating-environment failures — one costing real money. This entry is the incident response; **no costed run resumes until all three are cleared** (gate in the plan doc). Diagnosis was read-only; the verified root causes and the agent-vs-Sean fix split live in [`docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-02-operational-incidents-remediation-plan.md`](docs/anima-test-runs/2026-06-02-operational-incidents-remediation-plan.md).

**The three incidents (verified):**
1. **CRITICAL — API billed instead of subscription.** Confirmed against the [Claude Code auth doc](https://code.claude.com/docs/en/authentication): a present `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` outranks subscription OAuth, and *in non-interactive mode the `claude` CLI always uses the key when set*. anima's venv has `claude_agent_sdk 0.2.87`, so `sdk_runners.py` routes through the `claude` CLI → API-billed whenever the key is in the environment. **Corrected the source hypothesis:** anima's `.env` has NO `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` (verified), and `score.py`'s bare `load_dotenv()` can't add one that isn't there — the key was already exported in the **shell environment** (code-brain's `.env` carries it; a likely vector). The shell-side confirmation + re-auth are Sean's.
2. **agy reloads MCP servers per call.** Confirmed agy auto-loads the shared `~/.gemini/config/mcp_config.json` servers on every invocation; anima's vision path needs none. **Corrected the cost model:** this is local cold-start latency + child-process contention (the postmortem's no-traceback-exit contention), **not** Gemini token quota.
3. **Agents outlived the session.** Confirmed mechanism: `start_new_session=True` detaches a child from the terminal session, so it survives session end and can keep editing a shared tree. Current git state verified clean (`main @ 79d36f2`, single worktree, `stash@{0}` preserved); the live-process sweep is Sean's (sandbox can't see macOS processes).

**What landed this session (docs + code guardrails — no env/account changes):**
- **`evals/vision_critic/score.py` fail-fast guard** — refuses to start (`SystemExit(3)`) if `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is set, unless `--stub` or the new `--allow-api-key` override. Makes incident #1 structurally hard to re-run.
- **`.env.example`** — documents the auth policy (subscription via `claude login`/`setup-token`; never set `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`) and the non-Anthropic keys anima actually uses.
- **`docs/fleet-ops-protocol.md`** + a CLAUDE.md Source-of-Truth pointer — standing discipline: subscription-only billing, one isolated worktree per plan, singleton pre-flight + own-PID resolution, single owner, clean teardown (don't `start_new_session` a costed worker). Each rule tied to the incident it prevents.
- **`pipeline/agents/agy-config/mcp_config.json`** (`{"mcpServers": {}}`) + README — the MCP-free config anima's `agy` calls will point at (Option A, surgical). Wrapper wiring is pending one verification (`agy --help` for a config-dir override flag/env) — Sean's check, then a one-line `cli_runners.py` change.

**Still Sean's to do (account/shell-touching):** `unset ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` + remove the export from shell rc; `claude logout && claude login` (subscription); `claude setup-token` → `CLAUDE_CODE_OAUTH_TOKEN` for headless; disable API auto-reload; the positive billing-verification test (cheap real call → API dashboard stays flat); the live-process sweep; the `agy --help` config-override check; decide the fate of `stash@{0}`.

**Why:** stop the money leak first, prove the fix, make recurrence structurally hard — then the deferred Em re-baseline (23 performs + 1 motion smoke, false-pass-first) can finally run safely.
